Pariśiṣṭa nakṣatrakalpaḥ
AVParis śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ 
oṃ namo 'tharvātmane vāmadevāya śivāya 
śrīsarasvatyai namaḥ 
AVParis atha nakṣatrakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
AVParis kṛttikā rohiṇī mṛgaśira ārdrā punarvasū puṣyāśleṣā maghāḥ
phālgunī phalgunyau hastaś
citrā svātir
viśākhe anurādhā jyeṣṭhā mūlam
pūrvāṣāḍhā uttarāṣāḍābhijic chravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhā śatabhiṣaḥ pūrvaproṣṭhapadottaraproṣṭhapadau revaty aśvayujau bharaṇyaḥ 
AVParis ṣaṭ kṛttikā ekā rohiṇī tisro mṛgaśira ekārdrā dve punarvasū ekaḥ
puṣyaḥ ṣaḍ āśleṣāḥ ṣaṇ maghāḥ catasraḥ phalgunyaḥ pañca hasta ekā citrā ekā svātir
dve viśākhe catasro 'nurādhā ekā jyeṣṭhā sapta mūlam aṣṭāv aṣāḍhā eko 'bhijit tisraḥ
śravaṇaḥ pañca śraviṣṭhā ekā śatabhiṣā catasraḥ proṣṭhapadau ekā revatī dve aśvayujau tisro bharaṇyaḥ 
AVParis iti saṃkhyāparimitaṃ brahma 
 AVParis āgniveśyaḥ kṛttikā rohiṇy ānurohiṇī śvetāyinaṃ mṛgaśira ārdrā bārhadgavī vātsyāyanau punarvasū bhāradvājaḥ puṣyo jātūkarṇyo  
'śleṣā vaiyāghrapadyo maghāḥ 
pārāśaryau pūrve phālguṇyāv aupaśivyā uttare māṇḍavyāyano hastaś citrā gautamī kauṇḍinyāyanaḥ
svātiḥ kāpile viśākhe maitreyy anurādhā kauśikī jyeṣṭhā kautsaṃ mūlaṃ hāritayajñī
pūrvāṣāḍhā kāśyapy uttarā śaunako 'bhijid ātreyaḥ śravaṇo gārgyaḥ śraviṣṭhā dākṣāyaṇī
śatabhiṣag vātsyāyanyau pūrve proṣṭhapade āgastyāv uttare śāṅkhāyanī revatī kātyāyany
āv aśvayujau mātṛbhyo bharaṇyaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapa ādityaś candramā brahmāṇo nakṣatreṣu 
AVParis kṛttikā agnidevatyā rohiṇyāṃ tu prajāpatiḥ 
saumyaṃ mṛgaśiraṃ vidyān marutaś cātra daivatam 
AVParis rudrasyārdrāditeḥ punarvasū puṣye vidyād bṛhaspatim 
aśleṣāḥ sarpadaivatyā maghāsu pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ 
AVParis bhagas tu pūrvayoḥ phalgunyor aryamottarayor api 
haste ca savitā daivaṃ citrā tu tvaṣṭṛdaivatā 
AVParis svātau tu daivataṃ vāyur indrāgnī tu viśākhayoḥ 
anurādhāsu mitro vai jyeṣṭhāyām indramahādevau 
AVParis ahir budhnyaś ca mūlasya nirṛtiś cātra daivatam 
āpaḥ pūrvāsv aṣāḍhāsu viśve devās tathottare 
AVParis abhijid brahmadevatyaḥ śravaṇe viṣṇur ucyate 
śraviṣṭhā vasudevatyā śatabhiṣag varuṇendrayoḥ 
AVParis aja ekapād diśaś ca ādityaś ca tathottare 
revatī pūṣadaivatyā aśvinyām aśvinau smṛtau 
AVParis bharaṇyo yamadevatyā devatāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ 
AVParis kṛttikā maghā mūlaṃ ca tathā pūrvāṇi dvandvinām 
etāni purastādbhāgāny ahaḥpūrvāṇi jānīyāt 
AVParis ārdrāṃ śatabhiṣajaṃ svātim āśleṣā bharaṇīr api 
naktaṃbhāgāni bruvate jyeṣṭhayā saha brahmāṇam 
AVParis punarvasū viśākhe ca uttarāṇi ca dvandvinām 
rātrīm ubhayataḥ pakṣau bhajante yā ca rohiṇī 
AVParis mṛgaśiraḥ puṣyo hastaś citrā tu sahānurādhaiḥ 
śravaṇaś ca śraviṣṭhāś ca revaty aśvayujau nava 
AVParis etāny upariṣṭādbhāgāni rātrīpūrvāṇi jānīyāt 
muhūrto 'bhijid ucyate 
AVParis purastādbhāgāny anāgatenopariṣṭādbhāgāny atikrāntena ubhayatobhāgāni vartamānena naktaṃbhāgāni samaṃ candreṇa vā 
AVParis ṣaḍ anāgatayogīni sthitayogīni dvādaśa 
navātikrāntayogīni tathā yogaḥ pradṛśyate 
AVParis bahūni jātāni graho hinasti kṛttikāsu tiṣṭhann uta dīrgham āyuḥ 
ajāvayo mūṣikāś ca vyathante viśo brahmaṇaḥ saha mlecchavāṃś ca 
AVParis kaliṅgānāṃ vyathate nanu rājā hiraṇyakārāṃś ca nihanti kṛtsnam 
ayaskārā lohakārā āhitāgniś ca kṛtsnaṃ niyanti sahāgnitaptaiḥ 
AVParis ayo lohaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ hiraṇyamiśraṃ yac ca patanti sāram 
kāśāḥ kuśā yac ca suvarṇavarṇaṃ yac cāgnivarṇaṃ phalamūlapuṣpam 
AVParis ye tatra jātāḥ sarāṃsi śuṣyanty apayanti nadyaḥ prajā vyathante paśavo mṛgāś ca 
prajāpater hṛdaye pīḍyamāne sarvaṃ jagad vyathate sapradeśam 
AVParis mahābhaumo rājā mariṣyatīti vidyād ekāriṇāṃ chavakām invakāsu 
nakṣatrabhāge niyanti yojadhānāḥ tathā hi nūnaṃ triṇavena sṛṣṭam 
AVParis tathā sa ninye nidhānadarśanāya tatra teṣāṃ sahākṣemaṃ tasya vidyāt 
paritya ye pūrvapadān balena uttiṣṭhanti vīryavanto mṛgānām 
AVParis bhagena devy upayanti divyam ārdrābhāge sahino bhavanti 
tatra daivān mānuṣyāṃś ca punarvasvor nakṣatra bhāge niniyoja dhānāḥ 
AVParis tathā hi nūnaṃ puṣyo bhāga ekadhā brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā vidur nakṣatraveditāraḥ tathā hi nūnam 
AVParis śatadrayaḥ kaiśikā dakṣiṇārdhā āndhrāś ca yogahāsayā pravṛddhāḥ 
aśleṣābhāge sahino bhavanti tatra 
AVParis veṇūn pitṝṃs trirujāhur devatām 
maghābhāge aṣṭame devasṛṣṭam 
saṃyujyante devaprasādanena tatra 
AVParis rājñāṃ rākāyām atha madrakaikayā manomāpāyanasahaparisunniyojasahāntau 
tunyam atha saptamātraṃ pūrvabhāge navake phalgunīṣu 
AVParis matsyā māgadhāś cedayaś ca śālvā matsyā ubhe phalgunīṣu 
saṃyujyante devaprasādanena tatra 
AVParis pūrvācāryā icchamānāś ca sarve yakṛt kloma saha bhāgena haste 
saṃyujyante devaprasādanena tatra 
AVParis ye pūrvārdhe nijīhate carantaḥ śāntā mṛgā jantupaśavo apagāminas te 
paśavo bhavatāś ca sarve citrāyā bhāge sahino bhavanti  tatrā
AVParis cyutakeśaṃ vāhanaṃ jayārthaṃ kumāryo anaḍvān sahate atra ye 
vijñāyate devasṛṣṭaṃ purāṇaṃ svātiṃ bhajante tṛṇavaś ca sarve 
AVParis vṛkṣā vṛkṣamūlam ikṣvākavaś ca viśākhāyāṃ yojitāḥ sāṃpadena 
tasmin gṛhīte bhayam eva teṣāṃ daivopasṛṣṭe tu balena kāryam 
ye tatra jātāḥ 
AVParis ye paścārdhe nijīhate caranta āsavo mṛgā uttarārdhāś cāndhrāḥ 
anūrādhāsu magadhavaṅgamatsyāḥ sarve samagrāḥ sahino bhavanti tatra 
AVParis pañcaikadhā janapadā bhavanti sayujaḥkāsaubaladādauṣyadhāḥ 
bāhlīkā jyeṣṭhā upayanti bhaktyā tatra 
AVParis ikṣvākūṇāṃ nirmathyā mūlam āhuḥ 
tathā vidur nakṣatraveditāras tathā hi nūnam
AVParis kāmbojāḥ kālamṛṣāś ca krandā ucchuṣmāṇaḥ śvānaś cāvadhūmamarkaṭāś ca pūrvāṣāḍhā upayanti bhaktyā tatra 
AVParis viśve devāḥ saha pañcālajyeṣṭhā āpaś ca yāḥ pāntu bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyat 
uttarāṣāḍhā upayanti bhaktyā tatra 
AVParis nārkavindā nārvvidālā nasṛṅgāvau naiṣadhā jantavo mataṅgāḥ 
abhijitaṃ hārthavijñāya bhejire tatra 
AVParis pāñcālāḥ śravaṇam upaiti bhaktyā sunvantaś cobhe vidvān bhūtā niniyoja devaḥ 
pūrvakartā bhūtabhaviṣyakālas tathā ni nūnam
AVParis kurūn śraviṣṭhās tathā śivās tathāhur nakṣatrabhāge niniyoja dhānāḥ 
tathā hi nūnam
AVParis aṅgādayo janapadā guhāśayā apsu ca ye kṣipanti śatabhiṣaji bheṣajasya bhejire tatra 
AVParis khaḍgā hastino gavayā varāhā ahīnarā kuntayaś cāpi sarve 
pūrvau proṣṭhapadā upayanti bhaktyā tatra 
AVParis uśīnarā uttarayoḥ proṣṭhapadayor nakṣatrabhāge niniyoja dhānāḥ 
tathā hi nūnam
AVParis āvṛtāḥ śūdrāḥ saha kāravaś ca dakṣiṇapūrve yūkabhiḥ saha revatīṃ hārthavijñāya bhejire tatra 
AVParis acyutakeśaṃ vāhanaṃ ca padārtham ucāvacajanapadā mahāntaḥ 
aśvayujau hārthavijñāya bhejire tatra 
 AVParis ubhaye kīkaṭāḥ kauśalāś ca rahaś cavo ye ca prasuptāś caranti bharaṇīḥ sahārthavijñāya bhejire tatra teṣāṃ sahākṣayam asya  
vidyāt  
AVParis kariṣyamāṇaḥ saṃgrāmaṃ pratirājena kṣatriyaḥ 
brāhmaṇaṃ pūrvam anvicched vidvāṃsaṃ śāstravittamam 
AVParis utpātān yas tu yān vidyād divyāntarikṣapārthivān 
taṃ vai lipsitum arhati rājā rāṣṭre jijīviṣuḥ 
AVParis grahāṇāṃ yaḥ sthitiṃ vidyān nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca sāṃpadam 
anabhyaktam upāsīta nakṣatrasamatāṃ ca yat 
AVParis āyudhīyān bibhrad rājā kṛttikāsu na riṣyati 
tad dhi tejasvi nakṣatraṃ bahulaṃ divi rocate 
AVParis atho hi kṛttikā iti nakṣatraṃ bhānumattamam 
āgneyam agninakṣatraṃ rājā hy asmin pravardhate 
AVParis rohiṇyāṃ sārdham āsīta rajjupalyāni kārayet 
mṛgaśirasy aśvān bibhṛyāt sāsya senā na riṣyati 
AVParis saumyaṃ somasya nakṣatraṃ rājā hy asmin pravardhate 
ārdrāyāṃ mṛgayāṃ yāyād amitrebhyaś ca hāvayet 
AVParis punarvasvābhiyuñjīta puṣyenaitāṃ prayojayet 
iṣīkāṃ chedayan rājā aśleṣāsu na riṣyati 
AVParis maghābhiḥ sārdham āsīta na yāyād ucchrayaṃ cana 
phalgu dvārāṇi kārayet paricārāṃś ca vāhayet 
AVParis toraṇāni ca saṃhanyuḥ phalakāni ca takṣayet 
 uttarābhyāṃ ca hāvayet 
AVParis hastena citrām ākāṅkṣen nakṣatrasya parigraham 
anekadarśī syāc citrāyāṃ purā svāter abhiplavāt 
AVParis svātau śiśūn niyojayej javārthān rathavāhinaḥ 
athāsmin kanyām upavāsayet kṣipraṃ sā labhate patim 
AVParis pradatīn kārayan rājā viśākhāyāṃ na riṣyati 
lepayet pradatī rājā anūrādhāsu kṣatriyaḥ 
AVParis jyeṣṭhāyāṃ hastinaṃ paśyed abhiṣekāṃś ca kārayet 
 rājaputrāṃś ca yodhayet 
AVParis mūlena parikhāṃ khānayet puraṃ citena yojayet 
nairṛtaṃ rājanakṣatraṃ vadhyān anena ghātayet 
AVParis trirātraṃ sārdhaṃ dīkṣayitvā āṣāḍhāsu vrataṃ caret 
abhijity abhiyuñjīta śravaṇena cikīrṣatu 
AVParis śraviṣthābhiḥ sṛjed rasān 
AVParis śatabhiṣaji bhiṣakkarma bhaiṣajyaṃ cātra kārayet 
prācīnaproṣṭhapadayor yāyād 
AVParis uttarābhyām abhiyuñjīta gṛheṣu revatyāṃ vaset 
vi senāṃ kārayed rājā aśvinyāṃ bharaṇīṣu ca 
AVParis citrāṇi sākaṃ divi rocanāni sarīsṛpāṇi bhuvane javāni 
turmiśaṃ sumatim icchamāno ahāni gīrbhiḥ saparyāmi nākam 
AVParis suhavam agne kṛttikā rohiṇī castu bhadraṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śam ārdrā 
punarvasū sūnṛtā cāru puṣyo bhānur āśleṣā ayanaṃ maghā me 
AVParis puṇyaṃ pūrvā phalgunyau cātra hastaś citrā śivā svāti sukho me astu 
rādhe viśākhe suhavā anurādhā jyeṣṭhā sunakṣatram ariṣṭamūlam 
AVParis annaṃ pūrvā rāsatāṃ me aṣāḍhā ūrjaṃ dehy uttarā ā vahantu 
abhijin me rāsatāṃ puṇyam eva śravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhāḥ kurvatāṃ supuṣṭim 
AVParis ā me mahac chatabhisag varīya āme dvayā proṣṭhapadā suśarma 
ā revatī cāśvayujau bhagaṃ ma ā me rayiṃ bharaṇya ā vahantu 
 AVParis kṛttikā rohiṇī mṛgaśira ārdrā punarvasū puṣyāśleṣā maghāḥ pūrve phalgunyau tan navamam agnir daśamam ahorātre edādaśadvādaśe 
AVParis etāny evāsmai nakṣatrāṇi śriyaṃ bhūtiṃ puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ paśūn annam annādyaṃ samindhata iti veda
 AVParis atha yaṃ kāmayaty etāny evāsmai nakṣatrāṇi śriyaṃ bhūtiṃ puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ paśūn annam annādyaṃ samindhīrann iti tasmād etasmin  
nakṣatra evaṃvidvān kuryāt 
AVParis prāñcam idhmam upasamādhāya parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya
barhī rasān barhiṣy ādhāyānvālabhyātha juhuyāc citrāṇi sākaṃ divi rocanāni svāhety
agnau hutvā raseṣu saṃpātān ānīya saṃsthāpya homāṃs tata enaṃ prāśayati rasān 
AVParis evaṃ ced asmai karoty etāny evāsmai nakṣatrāṇi śriyaṃ bhūtiṃ puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ paśūn annam annādyaṃ samindhate 
 AVParis uttare phalgunyau hastaś citrā svātir viśākhe anūrādhā jyeṣṭhā mūlaṃ pūrvāṣāḍhā tan navamam ādityo daśamaṃ nāmarūpa  
pūrvapakṣāparapakṣāv ekādaśadvādaśe

AVParis ajany ajanir yaśo ajanir varco ajanis tejo ajaniḥ saho ajanir maho

vedānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarvāsāṃ sravantīnāṃ janitādhipatir ajanir bhavatīti veda

AVParis prāñcam idhmam  
 AVParis evaṃ ced asmai karoti sarveṣāṃ lokānāṃ sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vedānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarvāsāṃ sravantīnāṃ janitādhipatir  
ajanir bhavati  
AVParis viṣṭhitaśravā vai nāmaitan nakṣatraṃ yat pūrvāhne adhitiṣṭhati
vitiṣṭhaty asya puṇyā kīrtir ainaṃ puṇyā kīrtir gacchaty upainaṃ puṇyā kīrtis tiṣṭhati
nāsmāt puṇyā kīrtir apakrāmati kīrtimān prajayā paśubhiḥ śriyā gṛhair dhanena bhavatīti veda
AVParis atha yaṃ kāmayeta vitiṣṭhed asya puṇyā kīrtir ainaṃ puṇyā kīrtir
gacched upainaṃ puṇyā kīrtis tiṣṭhen nāsmāt puṇyā kīrtir apakrāmet kīrtimān prajayā
paśubhiḥ śriyā gṛhair dhanena syād iti tasmād etasmin nakṣatra evaṃvidvān kuryāt 
AVParis prāñcam idhmam upasamādhāya paristīrya barhī rasān barhiṣy ādhāyānvālabhyātha
juhuyād viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ svāhety agnau hutvā raseṣu saṃpātān ānīya saṃsthāpya
homāṃs tata enaṃ prāśayati rasān 
AVParis evaṃ ced asmai karoti vitiṣṭhaty asya puṇyā kīrtir ainaṃ puṇyā

AVParis varco vai nāmaitan nakṣatraṃ yan madhyāhnainaṃ varco gacchaty upainaṃ
varcas tiṣṭhati nāsmād varco apakrāmati varcasvī prajayā paśubhiḥ śriyā gṛhair dhanena bhavatīti veda
AVParis atha yaṃ kāmayetainaṃ varco gacched upainaṃ varco tiṣṭhen nāsmād
varco apakrāmed varcasvī prajayā paśubhiḥ śriyā gṛhair dhanena syād iti tasmād etasmin

 AVParis evaṃ ced asmai karoty ainaṃ varco gacchaty upainaṃ varcas tiṣṭhati nāsmād varco apakrāmati varcasvī prajayā paśubhiḥ śriyā

AVParis tejo vai nāmaitan nakṣatraṃ yad aparāhṇainaṃ tejo gacchaty upainaṃ
tejas tiṣṭhati nāsmāt tejo apakrāmati tejasvī prajayā paśubhiḥ śriyā gṛhair dhanena bhavatīti veda

Pariśiṣṭab kṛttikārohiṇīmadhye paippalādā mantrāḥ
AVParisb oṃ yad rājānaṃ śakadhūmaṃ nakṣatrāṇy akṛṇvata

AVParisb bhadrāham astu naḥ sāyaṃ bhadrāhaṃ prātar astu naḥ

AVParisb yad āhuḥ śakadhūmaṃ mahānakṣatrāṇāṃ prathamajaṃ jyotir agre

Pariśiṣṭa rāṣṭrasaṃvargaḥ
AVParis om  brahmaṇe brahmavedāya rudrāya parameṣṭhine

AVParis daivaṃ prabhavate śreṣṭhaṃ hetumātraṃ tu pauruṣam

Pariśiṣṭa purohitakarmāṇi
AVParis om atha purohitakarmāṇi

AVParis atha purohitaḥ snātānuliptaḥ śuciḥ śuklavāsāḥ soṣṇīṣaḥ savitā prasavānām iti vyākhyātam

AVParis paryaṅkam āsanaṃ khaḍgaṃ dhvajaṃ chattraṃ sacāmaram 
ratham aśvagajaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanur varma śareṣudhim 
AVParis āñjanaṃ gandhamālyāni vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca 
sarvān śāntyudakenaitān abhyukṣyec cābhimantrayet

AVParis yuṣmatprasādāc chāntim adhigacchāmīti 
AVParis tathāstv ity ukto nirgacched iti 
AVParis evaṃkṛtyasvastyayano yad evāvalokayati ta sidhyati 
AVParis tad api ślokāḥ 
AVParis asuraiḥ pīḍyamānas tu purā śakro jagatprabhuḥ 
kārayām āsa vidhivat purodhastve bṛhaspatim 
AVParis sa vṛto bhayabhītena śamanārthaṃ bubhūṣatā

bhūmiḥ siddhārthakāḥ sarpiḥ śamī vrīhiyavau tathā

AVParis suvarṇaniṣkaṃ kṛṣṇalaṃ vā vāmahastena saṃgṛhya

AVParis dhenuṃ cārogām
AVParis aparimitaguṇān tilān sauvarṇamaye tāmramaye vā pātre sthāpayitvā yad ajñānād ity abhimantrya viprāya dadyāt 
AVParis yad ajñānāt tathā jñānād yan mayā śabalaṃ kṛtam 
tat sarvaṃ tiladānena dahyatām iti hi prabho 
AVParis bhūmiś ca sasyasaṃpannā brāhmaṇe vedapārage

AVParis annaṃ tu vividhaṃ nityaṃ pradadyāt dvijātaye

dhūpena cānnapānena stotreṇa ca samarcayet

AVParis mamobhā mahyam āpa iti sūktābhyām anvālabhya japet

AVParis athāto rātrisūktānāṃ vidhim anukramiṣyāmaḥ 
AVParis śuciḥ śuklavāsāḥ purohitaḥ 
AVParis pārthivasya paścimāṃ saṃdhyām upāsya darbhaiḥ pavitrapāṇī rājānam abhigamya
AVParis piṣṭamayīṃ rātriṃ kṛtvā 
AVParis annapānadhūpadīpair arcayitvā mālyaiś ca

AVParis rājaveśmani dvāre visarjayitvā 
AVParis na taṃ yakṣmā aitu deva iti guggulukuṣṭhadhūpaṃ dadyād
AVParis yas te gandha iti bhūtim abhimantrya
AVParis tryāyuṣam iti rājñe rakṣāṃ kṛtvā

AVParis bhūtinā rakṣāṃ kṛtvā niṣkramya
AVParis evamevam aharahaḥ kuryāt 
AVParis yasya rājño janapade atharvā śāntipāragaḥ

AVParis yasya rājño janapade sa nāsti vividhair bhayaiḥ 
pīḍyate tasya tad rāṣṭraṃ paṅke gaur iva majjati 
AVParis tasmād rājā viśeṣeṇa atharvāṇaṃ jitendriyam 
dānasaṃmānasatkārair nityaṃ samabhipūjayet 
AVParis nityaṃ ca kārayec chāntiṃ grahaṛkṣāṇi pūjayet 
bhūmidohān prakurvīta devatāyataneṣu ca 
AVParis catuspatheṣu goṣṭheṣu tīrtheṣv apsu ca kārayet

Pariśiṣṭa puṣyābhiṣekaḥ
AVParis om atha puṣyābhiṣekasya vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi sāṃpadam 
dharmārthakāmasaṃyuktaṃ rājā kuryāt purohitam 
AVParis sauvarṇarājatais tāmraiḥ kalaśaiḥ pārthivair api 
sahasreṇa śatenātha toyagrahaṇam iṣyate 
AVParis caturṇāṃ sāgarāṇāṃ tu nadīnāṃ ca śatasya tu 
abhiṣekāya rājñas tu toyam āhṛtya yatnataḥ 
AVParis ekadvitricaturṇāṃ vā sāgarasya tu pañcamam 
oṣadhīs teṣu sarveṣu kalaśeṣūpakalpayet 
AVParis sahā ca dahadevī ca balā cātibalā tathā 
madayantī vacā śvetā vyāghradantī sumaṅgalā 
AVParis śatāvarī jayantī ca śatapuṣpā sacandanā 
priyaṅgū rocano aśīram amṛtā ca sasārikā 
AVParis aśvatthaplakṣabilvānāṃ nyagrodhapanasasya ca

AVParis hemaratnauṣadhībilvapuṣpagandhādhivāsitān

AVParis sāvitry ubhayataḥ kuryāc chaṃ no devī tathaiva ca

AVParis dharaṇī pādapīṭhaṃ syād dūrvāmūlāṅkurān śubhān

AVParis anaḍudvyāghrasiṃhānāṃ mṛgasya ca yathākramam

AVParis cāturhotravidhānena juhuyāc ca purohitaḥ 
caturdikṣu sthitair viprair vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ 
AVParis bilvāhāraḥ phalāhāraḥ payasā vāpi vartayet

AVParis gavyena payasā kuryāt sauvarṇena sruveṇa tu

AVParis śarmavarmā gaṇaś caiva tathā syād aparājitaḥ

AVParis etān pañca gaṇān hutvā vācayeta dvijottamān

AVParis puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvāsya ārambhaṃ kārayed budhaḥ

AVParis uccairghoṣa iti tūryāṇy abhimantrya purohitaḥ 
sarvatūryaninādena abhiṣikto hy alaṃkṛtaḥ 
AVParis siṃhāsanaṃ samāruhya pīṭhikāṃ vā yathākramam

AVParis mattadvipacatuṣkaṃ ca caturdikṣu prakalpayet

AVParis tatas tu darśanaṃ deyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ nṛpeṇa tu

AVParis āśiṣas te hi dāsyanti tuṣṭā janapadā bhuvi 
evaṃ prajānurajyeta pṛthivī ca vaśā bhavet 
AVParis purohitaṃ mantriṇaṃ ca senādhyakṣaṃ tathaiva ca 
aśvādhyakṣaṃ gajādhyakṣaṃ koṣṭhāgārapatiṃ tathā 
AVParis bhāṇḍāgārapatiṃ vaidyaṃ daivajñaṃ ca yathākramam 
yathārheṇa ca yogena sarvān saṃpūjayen nṛpaḥ 
AVParis rājyaṃ purohite nyasya śeṣāṇāṃ ca yathākramam 
sthānāntarāṇi cānyāni dattvā sukham avāpnuyāt 
AVParis dūrvāsiddhārthakān sarpiḥ śamīr vrīhiyavau tathā śuklāni caiva puṣpāṇi mūrdhni dadyāt purohitaḥ 
AVParis atharvavihito hy eṣa vidhiḥ puṣyābhiṣecane

Pariśiṣṭa piṣṭarātryāḥ kalpaḥ
AVParis om athātaḥ piṣṭarātryāḥ kalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
AVParis ahatavāsāḥ purastāt talpasya gomayena sthaṇḍilam upalipya
AVParis ahatavastreṇa siṃhāsanam avachādya 
AVParis yāṃ devāḥ prati nandantīti rātrim āvāhayet 
AVParis saṃvatsarasya pratimām iti piṣṭamayīṃ pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvodanmukhīm upaveśayet 
AVParis chattraṃ hiraṇmayaṃ dadyād āsanaṃ ca hiraṇmayam 
dadyāc chubhrāṇi vāsāṃsi śubhraṃ caivānulepanam 
AVParis śubhram annam atathā dadyāt prabhūtāṃś caiva modakān 
dhūpaṃ ca vividhaṃ nityaṃ pradīpāṃś ca prakalpayet 
AVParis ā mā puṣṭe ca poṣe cety etābhir upasthāya 
AVParis rakṣoghnair mantraiḥ sarṣapān abhimantrya
AVParis āvatas ta iti japan samantāt talpasyāvakīrya
AVParis ayaṃ pratisara iti pratisaram ābadhya śarkarān pratidiśaṃ kṣipet 
AVParis dhūpaśeṣaṃ rājñe dadyād 
AVParis abhayapradaṃ karma 
AVParis paścāt sarveṣu koneṣu dvimukhīm ekamukhīṃ vā 
sarvato vijayāṃ rakṣām ekāṃ vā teṣu caturmukhīm 
AVParis ekamukhīṃ vā sarvatrāpratirathajapa ity eke
AVParis sarvatra śarkarākṣepaś ceti 
AVParis gṛhītvā piṣṭarātriṃ tu veśmadvāre visarjayet
AVParis vanaspatir aso madhya iti guggulukuṣṭhadhūpaṃ dadyād
AVParis yas te gandha iti bhūtim abhimantrya
AVParis tryāyuṣam iti rājñe rakṣāṃ kṛtvā

Pariśiṣṭa ārātrikam
AVParis oṃ na suṣvāpa purā śakro dānavānāṃ purodhasā 
prayuktair auṣadhair yogair mantrāṇāṃ japahomataḥ 
AVParis praṇipatya bṛhaspatim atharvāṇaṃ puraṃdaraḥ 
dānavaiḥ paribhūto 'haṃ trāhi mām ity uvāca ha 
AVParis tato 'sāv evam uktas tu prabhūtabalavardhanam 
ārogyadaṃ bhūtikaraṃ kṣudropadravanāśanam 
AVParis ārātrikaṃ hi kartavyaṃ tasya trātum idaṃ tadā 
kṛtvā piṣṭamayaṃ dīpaṃ suvartisnehasaṃyutam 
AVParis ati nihaḥ prānyān iti dvābhyām enaṃ pradīpayet 
pātre sapuṣpe saṃsthāpya sarṣapāṃś ca sahākṣataiḥ 
AVParis priyaṅguṃ śatapuṣpāṃ ca dūrvāṃ caiva śatāvarīm 
sapāpahāriṇīṃ bhūtiṃ tatraiva ca baliṃ nyaset 
AVParis apsarobhiḥ parivṛto gurur gatvā puraṃdaram 
prāptasattvaṃ sumanasam āsane prānmukhaṃ sthitam 
AVParis preto yantv ekaśataṃ ca dīpaṃ samabhimantrayet 
triḥ paribhrāmayed rājño mantreṇātha sumaṅgalam 
AVParis śāmyanty asya tato rogā grahā vighnavināyakāḥ 
svasty astu nrparāṣṭrāya svasti gobrāhmaṇāya ca 
AVParis tatas tu śaṅkhadhvaninā dīpaṃ gṛhītvā satoyadhārāṃ prayato 'pi nirharet 
purohito jyotiṣiko 'pi vā svayaṃ hitaiṣinī dhātry atharvo pakāritā 
AVParis ācāmyātha ha rājānam ācamyādau purohitaḥ 
brāhmaṇāya yathāśakti rukmaṃ prātaḥ pradāpayet 
AVParis mūlakarmādikaṃ tasya pañcaguhyakakāritam 
bhayaṃ rājño na bhavati tejo vīryaṃ ca vardhate 
AVParis evaṃ vidhānam akhilaṃ vihitaṃ yathāvad etat samastaśubhadaṃ gaditaṃ nrpāṇām 
naivāpadaḥ samupayānti nṛpaṃ kadā cid ārātrikaṃ pratiniśaṃ kriyate tu yasya 
ity ārātrikaṃ samāptam 
Pariśiṣṭa ghṛtāvekṣaṇam
AVParis om atha ghrtāvekṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ 
 AVParis prātaḥprātaḥ śaṅkhadundubhinādena brahmaghoṣeṇa vā prabodhito rājā śayanagṛhād utthāyāparājitāṃ diśam abhiniṣkramyopādhyāyaṃ  
pratīkṣeta  
 AVParis atha purohitaḥ snātānuliptaḥ śuciḥ śuklavāsāḥ krtamaṅgalaviracitoṣṇīṣī śāntigṛhaṃ praviśya devānāṃ namaskāraṃ kṛtvā svastivācanam  
anujñāpya vinītavad upaviśet  
AVParis yamasya lokād yathā kalāṃ yo na jīvo 'sīti svastyayanaṃ kṛtvollikhyābhyukṣya paristīrya śantātīyena tilān ghṛtāktān juhuyāt
AVParis tān hutvā sauvarṇarājatam audumbaraṃ vā pātraṃ ghṛtapūrṇaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ
ghṛtasya jūtiḥ sahasraśṛṅgo yamasya lokād uru viṣṇo vi kramasvety abhimantryājyaṃ
teja iti tadālabhate 
AVParis ājyaṃ tejaḥ samuddiṣṭam ājyaṃ pāpaharaṃ param 
ājyena devās trpyanti ājye lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
AVParis bhaumāntarikṣadivyaṃ vā yat te kalmaṣam āgatam 
sarvaṃ tad ājyasaṃsparśāt praṇāśam upagacchatv iti 
AVParis tasmin ghṛtapātrasthaṃ hi sarvam ātmānaṃ ca paśyet 
AVParis dadhnā śiro hṛdayam anvālabhya japet 
AVParis uccā patantam iti dvābhyām
AVParis sūryasyāvṛtam iti pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya śeṣaṃ kārayed ity
AVParis atra ślokāḥ 
AVParis ayaṃ ghṛtāvekṣaṇasya prokto vidhir atharvaṇā 
upāsyo nityakālaṃ tu rājñā vijayakāṅkṣiṇā 
AVParis etat samāharet sarvaṃ prayatas tu samāhitaḥ 
rājā vijayate rāṣṭraṃ naśyante tasya śatravaḥ 
AVParis dvijottamāya kapilāṃ rājā dadyāt tu gāṃ śubhām 
āśīrvādaṃ tatas tena śrutvā tanmukhaniḥsṛtam 
AVParis guruṇā vācito yasmād dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt 
putrān pautrāṃś ca maitrāṃś ca labhate nātrasaṃśayaḥ 
AVParis āyuṣyam atha varcasyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ śatrutāpanam 
duḥsvapnanāśanaṃ puṇyaṃ ghṛtāsyāvekṣaṇaṃ smṛtam iti 
iti ghṛtāvekṣaṇaṃ samāptam 
śrīsāmba 
yamasya lokād adhy ābabhūvitha iti ṛcaḥ 
yathā kalāṃ yathā śapham iti ṛcaḥ 
ghṛtasya jūtir iti ṛcaḥ  ghṛtāvekṣaṇamadhye paippalādā mantrāḥ 
Pariśiṣṭa tiladhenuvidhiḥ
AVParis om atha tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanīm 
tilāḥ śvetās tilāḥ kṛṣṇās tilā gomūtravarṇakāḥ 
AVParis tilānāṃ tu vicitrāṇāṃ dhenuṃ vatsaṃ ca kārayet 
droṇasya vatsakaṃ kuryāc caturdroṇā tu gauḥ smṛtā 
AVParis suvāsāyāṃ śucau bhūmau dhūpapuṣpair alaṃkrtā 
kṛṣṇājine tu kartavyā bahūnāṃ vāpi kārayet 
AVParis karṇau ratnamayau kuryāc cakṣuṣī dīpakau tathā 
ghrāṇe tu sarvagndhāṃs tu jihvāyāṃ śāradaṃ ghṛtam 
AVParis danteṣu mauktikaṃ dadyāl lalāṭe tāmrabhājanam 
ūdhasi tu madhūśīram apāne ca ghṛtaṃ madhu 
AVParis hṛdaye candanaṃ dadyāj jaṅghayor ikṣukāṇḍakam 
suvarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurī raupyalāṅgūladakṣiṇā 
AVParis vastrachannā tu dātavyā kāṃsyapātraṃ tu dohanī 
AVParis prajāpatiś cety abhimantrya viprāya dadyāt
AVParis tatra ślokāḥ 
AVParis dhenuṃ vatsaṃ ca yo dadyād vinātharvābhimantritām 
vinānena vidhānena devatvaṃ nopajāyate 
AVParis viśvarūpāḥ sthitāḥ sarvā dhenavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
dhenutvaṃ na sa prayāti vinā sūktābhimantritām 
niṣphalaṃ naśyate sarvaṃ vinābhimantritaṃ satām 
AVParis bālatve yac ca kaumāre yat pāpaṃ yauvane kṛtam

AVParis yan niśāyāṃ tathā prātar yan madhyāhnāparāhṇayoḥ

Pariśiṣṭa rājakarmasāṃvatsarīyam

Pariśiṣṭab rājakarmasāṃvatsarīyam

Pariśiṣṭac vṛṣotsargaḥ
AVParisc atha vṛṣotsargaḥ 
 AVParisc kārttikeyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ raivatyām āśvayujyāṃ vā gavāṃ goṣṭhe paurṇamāsatantram ājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvā rudraraudrābhyām ājyaṃ

Pariśiṣṭab brahmayāgaḥ
AVParisb oṃ bhārgavaṃ praṇipatyātha bhagavāñ śaunako 'vadat

AVParisb paripṛṣṭaḥ sa tena atha atharvā yajatāṃ varaḥ 
vidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ pratiṣṭhāya ākhyātum upacakrame 
AVParisb sarveṣām eva yāgānāṃ paramo 'yam udāhṛtaḥ

AVParisb hṛdye manohare śubhre sarvābādhāvivarjite

AVParisb maṇḍapaṃ kārayet tatra yathoktavidhinā guruḥ

AVParisb puṣpaiś ca vividhaiḥ śubhraiḥ phalaiś ca api arcayed budhaḥ

AVParisb pradīpān ghṛtapūrṇāṃś ca pradadyād vividhān tathā

AVParisb sitacūrṇena tanmadhye likhet padmaṃ suśobhanam

AVParisb madhye padmaṃ tu saṃsthāpya brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaram

AVParisb tatha imā āpa ityā dyair yathāvad adhivāsayet

AVParisb ghṛtapradīpamālyaiś ca vastrair bhakṣaiś ca śobhanaiḥ 
sitacandanakarpūraṃ dadyād vā api hi guggulam 
AVParisb pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā namet sarvāṅgakair naraḥ 
dakṣiṇe paścime vā api bhāge vediḥ praśasyate 
AVParisb kṛtvājyabhāgaparyantaṃ tataḥ śāntyudakaṃ punaḥ

AVParisb hutvābhyātānamantrāṃś ca tato rudragaṇena ca

AVParisb homayet kutsasūktena ucchuṣmaiś ca yathāvidhi

AVParisb hutvā ca cātanaṃ tatra mātṛnāmagaṇena ca

AVParisb phalasnānaṃ ca kurvīta yukto maṅgalavādibhiḥ

AVParisb cārucāmarahastābhiś citradaṇḍaiḥ sadarpaṇaiḥ

AVParisb tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gataḥ 
āśāsyeṣṭaphalaṃ tatra yukto maṅgalapāṭhakaiḥ 
AVParisb tūryaghoṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ kṛtasvastyayanas tathā

AVParisb kuryād uttaratantraṃ ca sadasyān vācayet tataḥ 
bhojayec chaktitas tatra brāhmaṇān vedapāragān 
AVParisb dīnānāthāndhakṛpaṇān bhakṣabhojyair anekadhā 
annapānavihīnāṃś ca viśeṣeṇa prapūjayet 
AVParisb dattvā ca dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā dadyād gaṇabaliṃ niśi 
gṛhadevās tu saṃpūjyāḥ kāryaś cāpy utsavo gṛhe 
AVParisb yogino bhojayet paścād gṛhesu gṛhamedhinaḥ 
achedyās taravaḥ kāryāḥ prāṇihiṃsāṃ ca varjayet 
AVParisb bandhanasthāś ca moktavyā baddhāḥ krodhāc ca śatravaḥ 
abhayaṃ ghoṣayed deśe guruṃ ca paripūjayet 
AVParisb abhayaṃ sarvato dattvā iṣṭe ca parameśvare 
dīrgham āyur avāpnoti kṛtsnāṃ bhuṅkte vasuṃdharām 
AVParisb brahmayāgavidhiḥ kṛtsno bhaktānāṃ tu mayoditaḥ 
atharvaṇā surendrāya praṇatāya śubhecchayā 
AVParisb kṛtābhiṣekaḥ kṛtayāga eṣa kṛtāhhnikaḥ kṛtarakṣaḥ sureśaḥ 
atharvaṇo 'nugraham āśu labdhvā triviṣṭapaṃ virarājāsapatnam  iti 
Pariśiṣṭa skandayāgaḥ or dhūrtakalpaḥ
AVParis athāto dhūrtakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
AVParis caturṣucaturṣu māseṣu phālguṇāṣāḍhakārttikapūrvapakṣeṣu nityaṃ kurvīta 
AVParis śvo bhūte ṣaṣṭhyām upavāsaṃ kṛtvā prāgudīcīṃ diśaṃ niṣkramya śucau
deśe manohare noṣare maṇḍalaṃ trayodaśaratniṃ kṛtvā madhye maṇḍapasya sarvavānaspatyāṃ
mālāṃ kṛtvā ghaṇṭāpatākāsrajaḥ pratisaraṃ ca mālāpṛṣṭhe kṛtvā madhye darpaṇāṃś copakalpayitvā
tatra yaṃ vahanti hayāḥ śvetā ity āvāhayet 
AVParis yaṃ vahanti hayāḥ śvetā nityayuktā manojavāḥ 
tam ahaṃ śvetasaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yaṃ vahanti gajāḥ siṃhā vyāghrāś cāpi viṣāṇinaḥ 
tam ahaṃ siṃhasaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yaṃ vahanti mayūrāś ca citrapakṣā vihaṃgamāḥ 
tam ahaṃ citrasaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yaṃ vahanti sarvavārṇāḥ sadāyuktā manojavāḥ 
tam ahaṃ sarvasaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yasyāmoghā sadā śaktir nityaṃ ghaṇtāpatākinī 
tam ahaṃ śaktisaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yaś ca mātṛgaṇair nityaṃ sadā parivṛto yuvā 
tam ahaṃ mātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis yaś ca kanyāsahasreṇa sadā parivṛto mahān 
tam ahaṃ siṃhasaṃnāhaṃ dhūrtam āvāhayāmy aham 
AVParis āyātu devaḥ sagaṇaḥ sasainyaḥ savāhanaḥ sānucaraḥ pratītaḥ 
ṣaḍānano 'ṣṭādaśalocanaś ca suvarṇavarṇo laghupūrṇabhāsaḥ 
AVParis āyātu devo mama kārttikeyo brahmaṇyapitraiḥ saha mātṛbhiś ca 
bhrātrā viśākhena ca viśvarūpa imaṃ baliṃ sānucara juṣasva 
AVParis saṃviśasveti saṃveśayet 
AVParis saṃviśasva varaghaṇṭāpsaraḥstave yatra subhujo hi nirmitāḥ 
saṃviṣṭo me dhehi dīrgham āyuḥ prajāṃ paśūṃś caiva vināyakasena 
AVParis imā āpa iti gandhodakaṃ pādyaṃ dadyāt 
pratigṛhṇātu bhagavān devo dhūrta iti 
ṣat caiva hiraṇyavarṇā itīme divyo gandharva iti gandhān yas te gandha iti cemāḥ sumanasa iti sumanasaḥ 
priyaṃ dhātur iti 
AVParis vanaspatir aso medhya iti dhūpam 
yakṣyeṇa te divā agniḥ śukraś ceti dīpam 
yo viśvataḥ supratīka iti parṇāni 
AVParis prakṣālya haviṣy upasādayed dadhyodanaṃ kṣīrodanaṃ guḍodanaṃ mudgapayasamiśradhānyamodakāni
sarvagandhān sarvarsān udakapūrṇaṃ mūlapurṇaṃ puṣpapūrṇaṃ phalapūrṇaṃ rasapūrṇaṃ copakalpayitvā
AVParis indraḥ sītam ity ullikhya agne prety agniṃ praṇīya prajvalya prāñcam
idhmam upasamādhāya bhaga etam idhmam iti tisṛbhir etam idhmaṃ sugārhaspatya ity
upasamādhāya samiddho agnir iti samiddham anumantrayate 
 AVParis bhadram icchanto hiraṇyagarbho mamāgne varcas tvayā manyo yas te manyo yad devā devaheḍanam iti ṣat kāmasūktādayo daśa mahīpataye  
svāhā  
AVParis dhūrtāya skandāya viśākhāya pinākasenāya bhrātṛstrīkāmāya svacchandāya
varaghaṇtāya nirmilāya lohitagātrāya śalakaṭaṅkaṭāya svāheti hutvā agnaye prajāpataye
ye devā divy ekādaśa stheti anumataye agnaye sviṣṭakṛta iti ca 
AVParis śivāgnikṛttikānāṃ tu stoṣyāmi varadaṃ śubham 
sa me stuto viśvarūpaj sarvān arthān prayacchatu 
AVParis dhanadhānyakulān bhogān sa me vacanavedanam 
dāsīdāsaṃ tathā sthānaṃ maṇiratnaṃ surāñjanam 
AVParis ye bhaktyā bhajante dhūrtaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ ca yaśasvinam 
sarve te dhanavantaḥ syuḥ prajāvanto yaśasvinaḥ 
AVParis yathendras tu varān labdhvā prītas tu bhagavān purā 
dehi me vipulān bhogān bhaktānāṃ ca viśeṣata iti 
AVParis kāmasūktenopahāram upaharet 
AVParis upahāram imaṃ deva mayā bhaktyā niveditam 
pratigṛhya yathānyāyam akruddhaḥ sumanā bhava 
AVParis sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ 
bhavebhave nādibhave bhajasva māṃ bhavodbhaveti bhavāya namaḥ 
AVParis devaṃ prapadye varadaṃ prapadye skandaṃ prapadye ca kumāram ugram 
ṣaṇṇāṃ sutaṃ kṛttikānāṃ ṣaḍāsyam agneḥ putraṃ sādhanaṃ gopathoktaiḥ 
AVParis raktāni yasya puṣpāṇi raktaṃ yasya vilepanam 
kukkuṭā yasya raktākṣāḥ sa me skandaḥ prasīdatu 
AVParis āgneyaṃ kṛttikāputram aindraṃ ke cid adhīyate 
ke cit pāśupataṃ raudraṃ yo 'si so 'si namo 'stu ta iti 
AVParis svāmine namaḥ śaṅkarāyāgniputrāya kṛttikāputrāya namaḥ 
AVParis bhagavān kva cid apratirūpaḥ svāhā bhagavān kva cid apratirūpaḥ 
AVParis maṇiratnavarapratirūpaḥ 
kāñcanaratnavarapratirūpa iti 
 AVParis ete te deva gandhā etāni puṣpāṇy eṣa dhūpa etāṃ mālāṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇāṃ kṛtvā ādityakartitaṃ sūtram iti pratisaram ābadhnīyāt 
AVParis ādityakartitaṃ sūtram indreṇa trivṛtīkṛtam 
aśvibhyāṃ grathito granthir brahmaṇā pratisaraḥ kṛtaḥ 
AVParis dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam aśubhasya ca ghātanam 
badhnāmi pratisaram imaṃ sarvaśatrunibarhanam 
AVParis rakṣobhyaś ca piśācebhyo gandharvebhyas tathaiva ca 
manuṣyebhyo bhayaṃ nāsti yac ca syād duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam 
AVParis svakṛtāt parakṛtāc ca duṣkṛtāt pratimucyate 
sarvasmāt pātakān mukto bhaved vīras tathaiva ca 
AVParis abhicārāc ca kṛtyātaḥ strīkṛtād aśubhaṃ ca yat 
tāvat tasya bhataṃ nāsti yāvat sūtraṃ sa dhārayet 
AVParis yāvad āpaś ca gāvaś ca yāvat sthāsyanti parvatāḥ 
tāvat tasya bhayaṃ nāsti yaḥ sūtraṃ dhārayiṣyatīti 
AVParis anvāyaṃ bhuktvā devaṃ visarjayet 
AVParis pramodo nāma gandharvaḥ pradoṣo paridhāvati 
muñca śailamayāt pāpan muñcamuñca pramuñca ca 
AVParis yāvat imā āpaḥ pavanena pūtā hiraṇyavarṇā anavadyarūpāḥ 
tāvad imaṃ dhūrtaṃ pravāhayāmi pravāhito me dehi varān yathoktān 
AVParis uditeṣu nakṣatreṣu gṛhān praviṣṭo gṛhiṇīṃ paśyet dhanavati dhanaṃ me dehīti 
 AVParis yad bhoktuṃ kāmajātaṃ jagatyāṃ manasā saṃhīhate tattad dvijanmā pinākasenayajamānāt kāmam upabhukto bhuktvāmṛtatvaṃ tadvad  
evābhyupaiti  
Pariśiṣṭa saṃbhāralakṣaṇam
AVParis oṃ saṃbhārān kīrtayiṣyāmo yathālakṣaṇasaṃyutān 
yaiḥ karma kriyamāṇaṃ hi phalavat syād dvijanmanām 
AVParis achinnāgrān kuśān ārdrān indranīlasamaprabhān 
śuṣkān api śvetavarṇān āhuḥ śāntikarān budhāḥ 
AVParis surabhīṇi ca puṣpāṇi susvādūni phalāni ca manoharāṇi vāsāṃsi saṃbhāreṣūpakalpayet

Pariśiṣṭa araṇilakṣaṇam
AVParis om athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi araṇyoś caiva lakṣaṇam 
rūpam athā pramāṇaṃ ca guṇadoṣān tathaiva ca 
AVParis coditān śabdaśāstreṇa ācāryeṇa tu dhīmatā 
purā kalpe ca yad dṛṣṭam ṛṣibhiś caiva lakṣaṇam 
AVParis gṛhyāgniṃ parisaṃgṛhya dharmapatnyā sahaiva tu

AVParis tithau śubhāyāṃ nakṣatre diśaṃ gatvā tv aninditām 
aśvatthāt tu śamīgarbhād uktam āharaṇaṃ śruteḥ 
AVParis śamīvṛkṣe tu yo 'śvattho nānyavṛkṣeṇa saṃyutaḥ 
madhye mūlaṃ na bāhye tu sa garbhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
AVParis abhāve tu śamīgarbhe aśvatthād eva vāharet

araṇyoś cāṅgasaṃbhūtaṃ netraṃ cātraṃ ca pīḍakaḥ

Pariśiṣṭa yajñapātralakṣaṇam

Pariśiṣṭa kuṇḍalakṣaṇam

vāyavyāṃ pañcakoṇaṃ tu vāyavyeṣv api karman 
AVParis uttarasyāṃ tu padmābhaṃ saumyeṣv api ca karmasu 
aiśānyāṃ saptakoṇaṃ tu raudreṣv api yathoditam 
AVParis sarvakarmasu vijñeyaṃ kuṇḍaṃ padmanibhaṃ tu yat 
caturaśraṃ tu sarvatra samaṃ syād vijayāvaham 
AVParis sarvaśāntikaraṃ kuṇḍaṃ padmākāraṃ viśeṣataḥ 
śāntike caturaśraṃ ca pauṣṭike vartulaṃ tathā 
AVParis abhicāre trikoṇaṃ ca vaśyādau cārdhacandrakam 
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ māraṇādau ca vidveṣe cāṣṭakoṇakam 
AVParis mekhalā sarvakuṇḍeṣu dvādaśāṅgulam iṣyate 
caturaṅgulamānena pūrvāpūrvasamucchritā 
AVParis na cet purastād dhīnaṃ syāt sukhaṃ yajñaḥ samāpyate 
yat tu dakṣiṇato 'hīnaṃ tad rājñas tv abhayapradam 
AVParis yathāhīnaṃ paścimena bhavet tat siddhidaṃ śubham 
uttareṇa samamyat syāt tad rājño rājyavardhanam 
AVParis madhye samaṃ ca sukhadaṃ digvidikṣu samaṃ tu yat 
tad rājajanasaṃpatkṛt sarvāṃś cārīn vināśayet 
AVParis na cet purastād ityādi ya eṣa kathito vidhiḥ 
maṇḍapānāṃ gṛhāṇāṃ ca māne śāntikaraḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVParis hastakuṇḍaṃ sadāhome ayute dvikaraṃ smṛtam 
lakṣahome catuṣpāṇi koṭyām aṣṭakaraṃ smṛtam 
Pariśiṣṭa samillakṣaṇam
AVParis oṃ samidhāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śubham 
tathāśubhaṃ ca tattvena yathāphalavibhāgataḥ 
AVParis yajñakarmaṇi kartavyāḥ śāntike pauṣṭike tathā 
prādeśamātrīḥ samidhaḥ proktāḥ sarveṣu karmasu 
AVParis tiryag yavodarāṇy aṣṭāv ūrdhvā vā vrīhayas trayaḥ 
aṅgulasya pramāṇena prādeśo dvādaśāṅgulaḥ 
AVParis ata ūrdhvaṃ na kartavyā nāpi hrasvā na cordhvataḥ 
na vakrā caiva kartavyā nāpi granthisamanvitā 
AVParis ūrdhvatas tu yato vakrā citradadruvicarcikāḥ 
karoti yāge kṣipraṃ tu tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet 
AVParis dviphalā piṇḍavarjāpi triphalā vāpi yā bhavet 
ṣaṭphalā saptaphalā yā caturaṅgaṃ vinaśyati 
AVParis sapattrapuṣpasamidhaḥ kalpayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ 
pauṣṭikaṃ karma kurvīta sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
AVParis pattrapuṣpayutā yās tu śāntadrumasamudbhavāḥ 
samidho goṣṭhamadhye tu praśastāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
AVParis athāparaṃ pravakṣyāmi samidhāṃ caiva lakṣaṇam 
AVParis viśīrṇā dvidalā hrasvā vakrā caiva dvidhāgrataḥ 
kṛśā ca dīrghā sthūlā ca karmasiddhivināśinī 
AVParis yad yatra lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yasmin kāle yathāvidhi 
tatra tenaiva siddhiḥ syād viparīte tathā bhayam 
AVParis samāhṛtānāṃ samidhāṃ tāsāṃ caiva phalaṃ śṛṇu 
AVParis viśīrṇāyuḥkṣayaṃ kuryād dvidalā rogadā bhavet 
abhimukhagatamātrā sadyo hrasvā nivartayet 
AVParis durbhagaṃ kurute vakrā sthānabhraṃśaṃ dvidhāgrataḥ 
kṛśā sarvavināśāya dīrghā nāśayate śriyam 
AVParis sthūlā tu kurute vighnaṃ sarvakārye dvijasya tu 
ataḥ pramāṇaṃ vividhaṃ phalaṃ cāpi tathā śṛṇu 
AVParis latāpallavasaṃjātā dvādaśāṅgulakalpitā 
kṣīrāktā śāntike home hotavyā tu viśeṣataḥ 
AVParis kevalaṃ muktisiddhyarthaṃ ghṛtāktām homayeddvijaḥ 
daśāṅgulapramāṇāṃ hi homayen mantrakarmaṇi 
AVParis navāṅgulā tu kartavyā tailābhyaktābhicārike 
aṣṭāṅgulā vibhūtyarthe ghṛtadadhnā tu homayet 
AVParis kevalaṃ madhusaṃyuktā saptāṅguladalīkṛtā 
uccāṭane praśastā sā dvidalā ca na śāntaye 
AVParis vidveṣe kaṭutailāktā dvidalā tu ṣaḍaṅgulā 
sarvato granthihīnā tu viprāṇāṃ syāt samic chubhā 
AVParis avakrāgranthisaṃyuktā kṣatriyāṇāṃ jayāvahā 
madhye tu granthisaṃyuktā vaiśyānāṃ bhūtisādhanī 
AVParis trayāṇām api vakṣyante yā grāhyāḥ samidhaḥ smṛtaḥ 
nātyārdrā nātiśuṣkā vā naiva coṣarasaṃbhavāḥ 
AVParis na dagdhā na kṛmidaṣṭāḥ sarvadoṣavivarjitāḥ 
samidhām indhanānāṃ ca tulyān vṛkṣān bravīmy ataḥ 
AVParis śuṣukair yā indhanaiḥ pūrvaṃ yajñavṛkṣamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
ārdrāṇi homayec caiva śuṣkaiḥ kalahakarmaṇi 
śuṣkāṇi hīndhanāni syuḥ samidhas tu yathoditāḥ 
AVParis puṣṭikāmaḥ palāśasya gṛhṇīyāc chāntikarmaṇi udumbarasya vittārthī vaṭāśvatthasya rājyadhīḥ 
AVParis śrīkāmo bilvavṛkṣasya kadambasya tathaiva ca 
vidveṣaṃ kaṭukaiḥ kuryāt kaṇṭakair maraṇaṃ bhavet 
AVParis kakubhaṃ kaṭabhaṃ vṛkṣaṃ kauvirālaṃ tu kauhakam 
vaṃśaṃ vibhītakaṃ śigruṃ vidyād uccāṭane hitān 
AVParis stambhane sarvasainyānāṃ vijayārthe jayaṃ diśet 
apāmārgeṇa saubhāgyam āyuṣkāmo hi dūrvayā 
AVParis punnāgacampakau vṛkṣā ye cānye kṣīriṇaḥ śubhāḥ 
yad yatra lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yasmin kāle yathāvidhi 
AVParis tatra tenaiva siddhiḥ syād viparīte tathā bhayam 
arkaḥ palāśo madhuko nyagrodhodumbaras tathā 
AVParis plakṣo 'śvattho gomayānikuśāś ca samidhaḥ kramāt 
yathākrameṇa samidha ādityādigraheṣu ca 
AVParis śataṃ sahasraṃ lakṣaṃ vā gāyatryā paramāhutiḥ 
hūyamānaṃ tu yat kiṃ cit kṛtānnaṃ yadi vā tilāḥ 
AVParis grahanakṣatrapīḍāyāṃ sāvitryāpi hutaṃ hutam 
eṣabhedo mayākhyātaḥ śubhasya tv aśubhasya ca 
AVParis yathoktam etad yaḥ kuryāt sa sarvaphalam āpnuyād iti 
Pariśiṣṭa sruvalakṣaṇam
AVParis oṃ sauvarṇarājatais tāmraiḥ kāṃsyair draumais tathāyasaiḥ 
sruvaiḥ sarvaguṇopetaiḥ karma kuryād yathākramam 
AVParis sauvarṇai rājatair yajñe tāmraiḥ śāntikapauṣṭike 
kāṃsyena rudhiraṃ māṃsaṃ nānyaj juhuvīta kiṃ cana 
AVParis sarve yajñe prayoktavyā varjayitvāyasaṃ sruvam 
āyasaṃ khādiraṃ caiva abhicāre prayojayet 
AVParis adhunvaṃś caiva juhuyāt sruveṇāsphuṭitāhutim 
dhunvan hi hanti putrān tu rākṣasā sphuṭitāhutiḥ 
AVParis nānyat kiṃ cid abhidhyāyed uddhṛtyānyata āhutim 
tad daivatam abhidhyāyed āhutir yasya hūyate 
AVParis sruve pūrṇe japen mantram uttānaṃ śāntike karam 
śāntike pauṣṭike caiva varjayet tu kanīnikām 
AVParis nātidīrgho nātihrasvo nātisthūlaḥ kṛśas tathā 
aṣṭāviṃśatyaṅgulaḥ syāt kaniṣṭhāgrapramāṇataḥ 
AVParis dīrgho hinasti rājānaṃ hrasva rtvijaṃ vināśayet 
sthūlaḥ sasyopaghātāya kṛśaḥ kṣayakaraḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVParis gopucchāgrākṛtir daṇḍo maṇḍalāgram śiro viduḥ 
aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇena nimnaṃ śirasi khānayet 
AVParis etal lakṣaṇam uddiṣṭaṃ sruvasya phalabhedataḥ 
gopathena yathāśāstram uddhṛtaṃ śruticodanāt 
sruveṇa kurute karma hastenāpi tathā śṛṇu 
Pariśiṣṭa hastalakṣaṇam
AVParis oṃ yadā juhoti hastena dakṣiṇenetareṇa vā 
tadā vakṣye vidhiṃ tasya śreyasī syād yathāhutiḥ 
AVParis yathā naśyati caivāsya karma guhyam ajānataḥ 
tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi gopathaḥ pāṭham icchatām 
AVParis kuśabalbajamauñjāṃ vā kṛtvā veṣṭim anāmikām 
homakarma tataḥ kuryāt spṛṣṭvā vāmena dakṣiṇam 
AVParis na riktapāṇir juhuyān nānipātitajānukaḥ 
anipātitajānoś ca haranty āhutī rākṣasāḥ 
AVParis uddhṛtya samidho 'nnaṃ vā pañcabhir juhuyād budhaḥ 
śanaiś ca nirvaped annaṃ madhye 'gnau susamāhitaḥ 
AVParis gṛhakarmaṇi yajñe vā tathā pañcabhir eva tu 
śāntike pauṣṭike vaiva varjayet tu kanīnikām 
AVParis tisṛbhir juhuyād annaṃ na tilān naiva taṇḍulān 
yadābhicārikaṃ kiṃ cit tasmin kāle prayojayet 
AVParis vāmenābhicāran nityaṃ tribhir aṅgulibhiḥ samaiḥ 
nirdiṣṭaṃ tisṛbhiḥ śūlaṃ tena śatruṃ nipātayet 
AVParis apasavyena hastena savyaṃ yadi juhoti tat 
savyena cāpasavyaṃ tu savyaṃ yadi juhoti tat 
AVParis abhicāras tu tat proktaḥṣarvaśāntiṃ gamiṣyati 
Pariśiṣṭa jvālālakṣaṇam
AVParis oṃ bṛhaspatiṃ sukhāsīnam ātmavidyāparāyaṇam 
praṇipatya mahartvijaṃ nāradaḥ paripṛcchati 
AVParis kathayasva mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada 
aśubhaṃ yac chubhaṃ vāpi lakṣaṇaṃ pāvakasya tu 
AVParis sa pṛṣṭas tena tat sarvam ācacakṣe mahāmatiḥ 
AVParis hūyamānoyadā vahnir ṛjujvālaḥ pradṛśyate 
snigdhaś ca kiṃśukābhaś ca siddhis tatra vinirdiśet 
AVParis yatra bālārkavarṇābhaḥ karmaṇy agniḥ pradṛśyate 
śāntiṃ labhete tatrāśu yajamānapurohitau 
AVParis aśokakusumābho 'pi kāñcanābhas tathaiva ca 
śāntiṃ karoty ākālena hūyamāno hutāśanaḥ 
AVParis adhūmo jvalate kṣipraṃ kṛtvāvartaṃ pradakṣiṇam 
tadā śāntiṃ vijānīyād viparīte tathā bhayam 
AVParis śvasate garjate caiva visphuliṅgāḥ samantataḥ 
prāyaścittiṃ tadākuryād yad uktaṃ kauśikena tu 
AVParis athāpy āliṅgate bhūmiṃ bhramate ca samantataḥ 
aśubhaṃ kathayet tatra hotre 'sau pāvakaḥ svayam 
AVParis kapilaḥ piṅgalas tāmro raktaḥ kāñcanasaprabhaḥ 
śubhakṛt pāvako jñeyo viparīto bhayāvahaḥ 
AVParis yadāgnau lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ cid aśubhaṃ tu pradṛśyate 
hotā kleśam avāpnoti śāntiṃ tatra prayojayet 
Pariśiṣṭa laghulakṣahomaḥ
AVParis oṃ śaunakaṃ tu sukhāsīnaṃ gautamaḥ paripṛcchati 
lakṣahomasya yat puṇyam āhutīnāṃ ca devatāḥ 
AVParis tasmai yathāvad ācaṣṭe śaunako jñānalocanaḥ 
śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā lakṣahomaṃ yathāvidhi 
AVParis agnyāgārasya yā bhūmis tāṃ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ 
śuddhākṣārā samā snigdhā yā ca pūrvottaraplavā 
AVParis abhasmāsthyaṅgāratūṣā praśastā parikīrtitā 
pramāṇaṃ bāhumātraṃ tu jaṅghāmātraṃ dviratnikam 
AVParis caturaśraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ tulyaṃ sūtreṇa dhārayet 
brāhmaṇā vedasaṃpannā brahmakarmasamādhayaḥ 
AVParis upoṣya caikarātraṃ ca gāyatryā ayutaṃ japet 
upoṣya caiva gāyatryā japeyur ayutaṃ budhāḥ 
AVParis te śuklavāsasaḥ snātāḥ sragbhir gandhair alaṃkṛtāḥ 
nirāhārās tathā dāntāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ sajitendriyāḥ 
AVParis kauśam āsanam āsīnāḥ prayuñjyur homam uttamam 
ullikhya cādbhir abhyukṣya saṃskṛtya vidhipūrvakam 
AVParis agne praihy agninā rayim ity upasthāpya pāvakam 
kuryād upasamādhāya samās tvāgne samāhitaḥ 
AVParis lakṣahomakute pūrṇe dhenuṃ dadyāt payasvinīm 
anaḍvān kāñcanaṃ vastraṃ tuṣyeyur yena vā dvijāḥ 
AVParis yavais tu vipulān bhogān dhānyair āyuṣyam eva ca 
tilair hutvā tu tejasvī āyuḥ kīrtiṃ ca vardhate 
AVParis ādityaloko 'rkamayī pālāśī soma āpyate 
āśvatthī viṣṇulokasya brāhma audumbarī tathā 
AVParis anenaiva vidhānena hūyate 'tra hutāśanaḥ 
hutvaitāṃś caturo lakṣān brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati 
AVParis yāvaj jīvati kartāsau tāvat putrān dhanaṃ śriyam 
pūrṇe kāle vimānena nīyate paramaṃ padam 
Pariśiṣṭab bṛhallakṣahomaḥ
AVParisb om atha kāṅkāyano bhagavantam atharvāṇaṃ papraccha 
bhagavan kena vidhānena koṭihomaṃ lakṣahomam ayutahomaṃ vā prārambhamāṇaḥ katham ṛtvijo vṛṇīte kathaṃ ca kuryus tasmai sa hovāca 
AVParisb brāhmaṇo vā rājā vā vaiśyo vā grāmo vā janapado vā śrīkāmaḥ śāntikāmaḥ
koṭihomaṃ lakṣahomam ayutahomaṃ vāhaṃ kariṣyāmīti tasyā samāpter bhavadbhir amāṃsāśibhir
brahmacāribhir haviṣyabhugbhir bhavitavyam
 AVParisb tais tatheti uktaḥ kuṇḍam ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ caturhastam aṣṭahastaṃ vā samastahastaṃ vā dīrghaṃ vā daśahastaṃ khānayet  
tathā ca bādariḥ  
AVParisb lakṣahome tu kartavyam aṣṭahastaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
dvihastaṃ vā prakurvīta caturhastam athāpi vā 
AVParisb kuṇḍaṃ vā daśahastaṃ tu dvivistāraṃ tathottaram 
na cet purastād dhīnaṃ syāt sukhaṃ yajñaḥ samāpyate 
AVParisb atha dakṣiṇato hīnaṃ yajamānabhayaṃkaram 
paścimena vihīnaṃ syād yajñasyāsiddhidaṃ dhruvam 
AVParisb uttareṇa vinirdiṣṭaṃ rājño rājyaharaṃ bhṛśam 
madhye vihīnaṃ yad kuṇḍaṃ prajākṣayakaraṃ viduḥ 
AVParisb sraktihīnaṃ tu yat kuṇḍaṃ tad apy aśubhadaṃ bhavet 
dvādaśāṅgulamānena mekhalākṣetram ucyate 
AVParisb mekhalātrayam uddhiṣṭam ubhayaṃ caturaṅgulam 
caturaṅgulamānena pūrvāpūrvasamucchritā 
AVParisb prathamā sāttvikī proktā dvitīyā rājasī smṛtā 
tṛtīyā tāmasī jñeyā mekhalā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ 
AVParisb caturdaśāṅgulāṃ tatra yoniṃ kurvīta sādhakaḥ 
aṣṭāṅgulaṃ bhaved vṛttaṃ nirvāhas tu ṣaḍaṅgulaḥ 
AVParisb gajoṣṭhasadṛśākāra prājāpatyā ca sā ciduḥ 
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena kuṇḍaṃ lakṣaṇalakṣitam 
AVParisb sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvatas tu samāhitaḥ 
kuṇḍaṃ siddhikaraṃ jñeyam āyuḥkīrtivivardhanam 
AVParisb tasmād yatnena kuṇḍaṃ khātvādbhir abhyukṣya purastād agner ādityādīn
grahān pratiṣṭhāpyottarataḥ kṛttikādīni nakṣatrāṇi svāsu dikṣu lokapālān sarvāsu
kuṇḍasraktiṣv agnyādidevān ratiṣṭhāpya
AVParisb teṣāṃ pratimantram āvāhanādikaṃ kṛtvā vilīnapūtam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā
sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca saṃmṛjya pratapyedhmam upasamādhāyānvārabdhāya vāstoṣpatyādibhiś
caturbhir gaṇaiḥ śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ kartāram ācāmayati ca saṃprokṣati ca 
AVParisb atha samidho ghṛtāktās tilān vā svāhākāravatīḥ saṃkhyāvatyo gāyatryā mahāvyāhṛtibhir vā sarva ṛtvijo juhvati 
AVParisb śrīparṇamiśrāḥ śrīkāmasya śamīparṇamiśrāḥ śāntikāmasya karīrasaktumiśrā vṛṣṭikāmaysa badarādiphalamiśrāḥ paśukāmasya 
 AVParisb aharahaḥ karmaṇo 'pavargād atha pūrṇāyāṃ koṭyāṃ lakṣe vāyute vānvārabdhe yajamāne niśi mahābhiṣEkaṃ kṛtvā vasor dhāraṃ juhvati 
AVParisb audumbarīṃ srucaṃ śuraḥpramāṇāṃ brāhmaṇasya lalātapramāṇāṃ kṣatriyasya skandhapramāṇāṃ vaiṣyasyāpramāṇāṃ janapadasya
AVParisb teṣām ante saraṇārthaṃ nimnaṃ khānayitvoṣṇodakena prakṣālyājyam ānīya vasor dhārāṃ vaiśvānaraṃ prāpnoti 
AVParisb tad yad ājyadhānīṃ ca vaiśvānaraṃ prāpnoti athoccārayati 
AVParisb ojaś ca me kṣatraṃ ca me ye agnayo amo devavadhebhyo bhavāśarvau
mṛḍataṃ prāṇāya nama iti hutvā arghaṃ pradāya vastraṃ lodhraṃ mālyaṃ phalādīni bhājane
kṛtvā namas te astu paśyata iti svāhākāreṇāgnau prakṣipya yamyaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate so
'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate 
 AVParisb samṛddhihomādi samānaṃ svastyayanāni japet puṇyāhaṃ vācayed gobhūtilasuvarṇaṃ vāsaś ca rtvigbhyaḥ saṃpradāya praṇipatya visarjayet 
AVParisb tasminn ahani vyatīte yadi strī mālyahastā śvetacandanāniliptā
śvetapuṣpāṇy ādāya prayacched gaurasarṣapān pāṇyādhāre vā gṛhītvā prāsādam ārohayet
kuñjaraṃ vā pramattam aśvaṃ śvetaṃ vā parvataṃ govṛṣaṃ vā yānaṃ yuktaṃ vājibhir yady
ārohet svapnakāle samastasiddhiṃ vidyān manaso yām abhīṣṭām 
AVParisb tasmāt tāṃ rātrīṃ prayataḥ svapet 
svapnaṃ dṛṣṭvā rtvigbhyo nivedayet 
paro 'pehi yo na jībo 'si vidma te svapna yathā kalāṃ yathā śapham iti rājamukham abhimantrya yathāgataṃ gaccheyus tad api ślokāḥ 
AVParisb divyāntarikṣabhaumeṣu adbhuteṣu na saṃśayaḥ 
koṭihomaṃ viduḥ prājñā lakṣaṃ vāyutam eva vā 
AVParisb avijñātaṃ ca yat pāpaṃ sahasā caiva yat kṛtam 
tat sarvaṃ lakṣahomasya karaṇād dhi vinaśyati 
AVParisb tasmāt sarveṣu kāryeṣu śāntikeṣu viśeṣataḥ 
yaḥ kuryāt prayato nityaṃ na so 'narthān samaśnute 
Pariśiṣṭa koṭihomaḥ
AVParis oṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaś caiva pīḍyamānā mahāsūraiḥ 
mṛtyunā vyādhibhiś caiva brahmāṇam idam abruvan 
AVParis karmaṇā kena deveśa mṛtyur vyādhiś ca jīyate 
aiśvaryaṃ prāpyate vāpi sthānaṃ ca paramaṃ prabho 
AVParis evam ukto mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
pratyuvāceśvaraḥ sarvān viprān devagaṇaiḥ saha 
AVParis śṛṇudhvaṃ prayatāḥ sarve prāpyate yena karmaṇā 
aiśvaryam āyur ārogyaṃ putrā vijaya eva ca 
AVParis savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha 
ye japanti sadā tebhyo na bhayaṃ vidyate kva cit 
AVParis tayā homaś ca kartavyaḥ satataṃ siddhim icchatā 
yavais tilaiḥ samidbhiś ca vrīhibhiḥ sarṣapais tathā 
AVParis atha cen mahatīṃ siddhiṃ prārthayedhvaṃ surottamāḥ 
purodhasā kārayadhvaṃ koṭihomaṃ mahāphalam 
AVParis yādṛśaṃ kṛtavān pūrvam atharvā tryambakasya tu 
tādṛśena vidhānena koṭihomaḥ prayujyate 
AVParis mahattvaṃ prārthayamānaḥ śarvo 'tharvāṇam abravīt 
kuruṣva mama tat karma mahattvaṃ yena labhyate 
AVParis aiśvaryam āyur ārogyaṃ sthānaṃ ca paramaṃ prabho 
putrā lakṣmīr yaśo medhā balaṃ pauruṣyam eva ca 
AVParis evam ukto mahātejā atharvā mantradarśavit 
gāyatrīṃ tapasā yuktām ṛcaḥ padam itīti ha 
AVParis ṛcaḥ padaṃ mātrayeti mantre vijñāyate hi sā 
 gāyatrī vai tripād brahma viśvarūpā ca saṃsthitā 
AVParis prāṇadā sarvabhūtānāṃ dhāraṇī yāpi nityaśaḥ 
iti niścitya manasā koṭihomaṃ prayojayat 
AVParis samidbhiḥ śāntavṛkṣasya gāyatryā susamāhitaḥ 
tato mahattvam agamad aiśaryaṃ paramaṃ tathā 
AVParis mahādeva iti cāsya nāma lokeṣu viśrutam 
upadravāś ca ye ke cid upaghātās tathaiva ca 
sarve 'sya praśamaṃ yātāḥ skandaṃ putraṃ ca labdhavān 
AVParis tataḥ prītas tu bhagavāñ śaṃkaraḥ paryapṛcchata 
atharvāṇaṃ mahāprājñaṃ koṭihomasya ko vidhiḥ 
AVParis caturviṃśākṣaraṃ brahma tripādaṃ lokadhāraṇam 
sāvitraṃ tena homo 'yaṃ kṛto me koṭisaṃmitaḥ 
AVParis vidhiṃ cāsya pravakṣyāmi sarvalokahitāya vai 
yatprayogād bhavec chāntir vṛddhiś ca paramā nṛṇām 
AVParis upadraveṣu bhūtānām āpatsu vividhāsu ca 
koṭihomaḥ prayoktavyaḥ ketūnāṃ darśane tathā 
AVParis upasargabhaye caiva paracakrabhaye tathā 
anāvṛṣṭibhaye caiva koṭihomaṃ prayojayet 
AVParis ārambhaṃ tasya kurvīta śukle cāpi tithau śubhe 
muhūrte vijaye caiva tithichidrāṇi varjayet 
AVParis rohiṇyāṃ vaiṣṇave tvāṣṭre pauṣṇe maitrottareṣu ca 
abhijitpuṣyasaumyeṣu kuryāt puṇyeṣu vā budhaḥ 
AVParis atha cet tvarate kartuṃ koṭihomaṃ mahāphalam 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvāsya ārambhaṃ kārayed budhaḥ 
AVParis aṣṭahastaṃ tu nirdiṣṭaṃ koṭihomasya khātakam 
tasyaivārdhapramāṇena lakṣahome vidhīyate 
AVParis trirātropoṣito brahmā kṛtvā śāntiṃ caturgaṇīm 
prokṣayet karmasiddhyarthaṃ vāstu śāntyudakena tu 
AVParis mahāśāntividhānena nirmathyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ 
tāvat kuryād budhaḥ sarvaṃ yāvan no nairṛtaṃ kṛtam 
AVParis tataḥ prabhāte bahuśa uddhṛtyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ 
nirmathya hāvayet tatra samidho brāhmaṇān bahūn 
AVParis śataṃ sahasraṃ koṭiṃ vā viṃśatir daśa vā dvijāḥ 
juhuyuḥ śāntavṛkṣasya samidho ghṛtasaṃyutāḥ 
AVParis svayaṃ vāpi yajed brahmā savitāraṃ dinedine 
pākayajñavidhānena mantraś cātra viṣāsahim 
AVParis śāntikāmo yavaiḥ kuryāt tilaiḥ pāpāpanuttaye 
samidbhiḥ sarvakāmas tu bilvaiḥ prāpnoti kāñcanam 
AVParis labhate śriyam agryāṃ tu padmais tejo ghṛtena tu 
dadhnā tu labhate putrān payasā brahmavarcasam 
AVParis haviṣyabhojino dāntāḥ śuklāmbaradharās tathā 
hāvakā niyatāḥ sarve bhaveyur brahmacāriṇaḥ 
AVParis āraṇyam upayuñjānaḥ payasā vāpi vartayet 
phalāhāro 'pi vā brahmā koṭihomaṃ samācaret 
AVParis pratyekaṃ caiva hotṝṇāṃ dātavyā dakṣiṇā tataḥ 
niṣko aśvo gaur vāsaś ca hiraṇyaṃ vāpi śaktitaḥ 
AVParis yaś caivāpi bhaved brahmā prayoktā sarvakarmaṇām 
sarvasvaṃ tasya deyaṃ syād dhiraṇyaṃ vāpi tatsamam 
AVParis koṭihome samāpte tu yajed grahagaṇān budhaḥ 
kārayed amṛtāṃ caiva ghṛtakambalam eva ca 
AVParis kāryāmṛtā mṛtyubhaye ghṛtakambalasaṃyutā 
paracakrāgame tv aindrī ghṛtakambalam eva ca 
AVParis raudrī sarvādbhutotpattau ghṛtakambalasaṃyutā 
salilā salilakṣaye ghṛtakambala eva ca 
AVParis ghṛtakambalapṛṣṭhā ca salilā salilakṣaye 
yenayena tu kāmena koṭihomaṃ prayojayet 
AVParis āmnātaṃ tatra yat karma tad ante kārayed budhaḥ 
eṣa eva vidhir dṛṣṭo abhicāre vidhīyate 
AVParis pratilomayātra homaḥ sāvitryā tilasarṣapaiḥ 
ārambhaṃ tasya ghoreṣu nakṣatreṣu dineṣu ca 
AVParis kārayet kṛṣṇapakṣasya tithichidreṣu sarvadā 
maghāśleṣā tathā mūlaṃ revaty ārdrā ca sarvadā 
AVParis darbhārthe tu śarān kuryād ghṛtārthe tailam ucyate 
svāhākāre tu phaṭkāro veṇyādyāḥ syuś caturdaśa 
AVParis cāṇḍālāgnau citāgnau vā sūtikāgnāv athāpi vā 
hāvayed ghoravṛkṣāṇāṃ samidhas tailasaṃyutāḥ 
AVParis raktoṣṇīṣī raktavāsāḥ kṛṣṇāmbaradharo 'pi vā 
juhuyād vāmahastena samidho dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ 
AVParis khādirāgnau madhūcchiṣṭe kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ ripoḥ 
tāpayet pratilomāṃ tu sāvitrīṃ manasā japet 
AVParis kaṇṭhe śūlārpitāṃ kṛtvā tāpayet tu dinedine 
yāvac chatrur vaśaṃ yāti vilīnāyāṃ vinaśyati 
AVParis evaṃproktavidhānena koṭihomasya śaṃkaraḥ 
prītimān ucyate yena tac chubhaṃ bhautikaṃ dadau 
AVParis atharvā bhautikaṃ labdhvā śiṣyebhyas tat punar dadau 
śubhaṃ mokṣakaraṃ puṇyaṃ priyaṃ paśupater vratam 
AVParis etaj jñātvā tu yaḥ samyak koṭihomaṃ prayojayet 
sarvān kāmān avāpnoti brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati 
AVParis yas tv imaṃ śrāvayed vidvān paṭhate caiva sarvadā 
koṭihomaphalaṃ labdhvā rudraloke mahīyate 
AVParis gopathāt pāṇineyāya madhye nṝṇāṃ pramodinām 
hitārtham uddhṛto granthaḥ koṭihomas tu viśrutaḥ 
Pariśiṣṭa gaṇamālā
AVParis oṃ bhūs tat savituḥ śaṃ no devīḥ śāntā dyauḥ śaṃ na indrāgnī śaṃ no vāto vātu uṣā apa svasus tama iti śāntigaṇaḥ 
AVParis kṛtyāpratiharaṇo dūṣyā dūṣir asi īśānāṃ tvā samaṃ jyotir uto asy abandhukṛd
ye purastāt suparṇas tvā yāṃ te cakruḥ pratīcīnaphalo yad duṣkṛtam ayaṃ pratisaro
yāṃ kalpayantīti kṛtyāpratiharaṇāni 
iti kṛtyāgaṇaḥ 
AVParis cātanaḥ stuvānam idaṃ havir ye 'māvāsyām upa prāgān niḥsālām arāyakṣayaṇaṃ
śaṃ no devī pṛśniparṇy ā paśyati tānt satyaujās tvayā pūrvaṃ purastād yukto antardāve
juhuta prāgnaye rakṣohaṇam ity anuvākaś cātanāni 
iti cātanagaṇaḥ 
AVParis mātṛnāmā divyo gandharva ā paśyatīmaṃ me agne yau te māteti mātṛnāmāni 
iti mātṛgaṇaḥ 
AVParis vāstoṣpatīya āśānām āśāpālebhya ihaiva dhruvām ṛdhaṅmantro yonim uta
putraḥ pitaram indrasya gṛho 'sīti catasro dive svāhāśamavarma me pṛthivyai śrotrāyeti
dhanvānīti dve ūrjaṃ bibhrad iti ṣaṭsatyaṃ bṛhad ity anuvāko vāstoṣpatīyāni 
iti vāstugaṇaḥ 
AVParis pāpmahā vi devā jarasāvṛtam apa naḥ śośucad agham ava mā pāpmann iti pāpmahā 
iti pāpmahā gaṇaḥ 
AVParis takmanāśano jarāyujaḥ prathamo yad agnir ud agātāṃ daśavṛkṣa muñca
kṣetriyāt tvā hariṇasya raghuṣyado muñcāmi tvā bhavāśarvau manve vāṃ yo giriṣu dive
svāhāgnis takmānam agner ivāsyāva mā pāpmant sṛjāva jyām iva varaṇo vārayātā imaṃ
yavaṃ vidradhasya balāsasya namo rūrāyeti dve śīrṣaktiṃ śīrṣāmayam iti takmanāśanāni 
iti takmanāśanagaṇaḥ 
AVParis duḥsvapnanāśanāni dauṣvapnyaṃ daurjīvityaṃ paro 'paihi yo na jīvo
'si pary āvarte duṣvapnyād yat svapne annam aśnami yo na stāyad dipsati yo naḥ suptāṃ
jāgrato yan me manso duṣvapnyaṃ kāma svapnaṃ suptvā vidma te svapneti trayaḥ paryāyā
duḥsvapnanāśanāni 
iti duḥsvapnanāśanagaṇaḥ 
AVParis āyuṣyo yathā dyauḥ prāṇāpānāv ojo 'si tubhyam evākṣībhyāṃ te muñcāmi
tvota devā āvatas ta upa priyam antakāya mṛtyava ā rabhasva prāṇāya namo viṣāsahim ity āyuṣyāṇi 
iti āyuṣyagaṇaḥ 
AVParis varcasyo ye triṣaptā asmin vasu prātar agniṃ hastivarcasaṃ siṃhe
vyāghre yaśo havir yaśasaṃ mendro girāv aragarāṭeṣu yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane yac
ca varco akṣeṣu yena mahānaghnyā jaghanam iti varcasyāni 
iti varcasyagaṇaḥ 
AVParis svastyayano amūḥ pāre pātaṃ na indrāpūṣaṇā tvaṣṭā me daivyaṃ yena
soma namo devavadhebhyo 'bhayaṃ mitrāvaruṇāv upa prāgāt sahasrākṣo 'namitraṃ no adharād
yamomṛtyur bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu tyam ū ṣu trātāram indraḥ sutrāmā sa sutrāmā
ā mandrair indra marmāṇi te varma me dyāvāpṛthivī aindrāgnaṃ varma girayas te yat
te madhyaṃ yās te prācīr mā naḥ paścād iti svastyayanāni 
iti svastyayanagaṇaḥ 
AVParis abhayaḥ svastidā viśāṃ brāhmaṇena paryuktāsi na tā arvā reṇukakāṭo
abhayaṃ mitrāvaruṇāv abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī asmai grāmāya hataṃ tardaṃ pūṣemā āśā indraḥ
sutrāmā maitaṃ panthāṃ svastidā viśāṃ patir nama te ghoṣiṇībhya ā te rāṣṭram idam
uc chreyo yata indra bhayāmaha ity abhayāni 
ity abhayagaṇaḥ 
AVParis aparājito vidmā śarasya mā no cidann adārasṛt svastidā saṃśitaṃ me
tvayā manyo yas te manyo etā devasenā avamanyur nirhastaḥ pari vartmāny abhibhūr
indro jāyaty abhi tvendrety aparājitāni 
ity aparājitagaṇaḥ 
AVParis śarmavarmā yaḥ sapatna itaś ca yad amutaś cāpendra dviṣato yūyaṃ
naḥ pravata imam agna āyuṣe tisro devīr uruvyacā no indrasya śarmāsīti uttamāṃ varjayitvā
yena devā asurāṇām anaḍudbhyas tvam iti dve tanūṣ ṭe vājin vājasya nu prasave devānāṃ
patnīr adhi brūhi rakṣohaṇaṃ vājinaṃ ye srāktyaṃ varma me dyāvāpṛṭhivī aindrāgnaṃ
varma bahulaṃ varma mahyam ayaṃ mitraḥ pṛthivyod akrāmad aspatnaṃ purastād iti śarmavarmā 
iti śarmavarmā gaṇaḥ 
AVParis devapurā ye purastād brahma jajñānaṃ sahasradhāra evāgnir mā pātu
agniṃ te vasuvantaṃ mitraḥ pṛthivyod akrāmad apa ny adhuḥ pauruṣeyaṃ vadhaṃ jitam
asmākam iti devapurīyaḥ 
iti devapurīyagaṇaḥ 
AVParis rudro ye 'syāṃ prācī dig itirudragaṇaḥ 
iti rudragaṇaḥ 
AVParis raudro rudra jalāṣabheṣaja ye 'syāṃ prācī dig ud itas trayo akraman
bhavāśarvau manve vāṃ brahma jajñānam anāptā ye sahasradhāra eva grīṣmo hemanto anaḍudbhyas
tvaṃ mahyam āpo vaiśvānaro yamo mṛtyur yāṃ te rudra yo agnau rudro bhavāśarvau mṛḍataṃ
bhavāśarvāv idaṃ brūmo yas te sarpo vṛścikas tasmai prācyā diśo antardeśād iti raudragaṇaḥ 
iti raudragaṇaḥ 
AVParis citrāgaṇo mā no vidann adārasṛt svastidā viśām amūhoāre aghadviṣṭā
agne yat te tapa iti pañca sūktāni rudra jalāṣabheṣaja ye 'syāṃ prācī dig vi devā
uta devā agner manva itiprabhṛtīni mṛgārasūktāny uttamaṃ varjayitvāpa naḥ śośucad
aghaṃ pṛthivyām agnaye mamāgne vrahma jajñānam anāptā ye sahasradhāre savitā prasavānāṃ
nava prāṇān pātaṃ nas tvaṣṭā me yena soma namo devavadhebhyo 'bhayaṃ mitrāvaruṇāv
upa prāgāt sahasrākṣaḥ siṃhe vyāghre 'bhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī grīṣmo hemanto 'naḍudbhyas
tvaṃ mahyam āpo vaiśvānaro yamo mṛtyur abhi tvendra viśvajit trāyamāṇāyai imaṃ me
agne viṣāṇā pāśān śakadhūmaṃ somārudreti dve bṛhaspatir nas tyam ū ṣu trātāram indraḥ
sutrāmā ā mandrair indra marmāṇi te antakāya mṛtyavā ā rabhasvāyaṃ pratisaro 'yaṃ
me varaṇo bhavāśarvau mṛḍataṃ prāṇāya namo 'gniṃ brūma ity arthasūktaṃ satyaṃ bṛhad
iti dve prathame girayas te yat te madhyaṃ yās te prācīr mā naḥ paścād grīṣmas te
bhūme varṣāṇy upasthās te bhūme mātaḥ sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho jātavedā mā pra gāma patho
yo yajñasya tasmai prācyā diśo antardeśād iti paryāyaś citrāgaṇaḥ 
iti citrāgaṇaḥ 
AVParis patnīvanto aditir dyauḥ sinīvāli kuhūṃ devīm iti trīṇi sūktāni patnīvantaḥ 
iti patnīvantagaṇaḥ 
AVParisb svasti mātra indra juṣasvāyā viṣṭhā śive te stāṃ pādābhyāṃ te saṃ
te śirṣṇo vatso virāja ity ekā uccā patantam iti dve bhūyān indro viṣāsahiṃ sahamānam ity ādityagaṇaḥ 
AVParis śaṃ no devī śaṃ na indrāgnī śaṃ no vāto vātu śāntā dyauḥ pippalādiśāntigaṇaḥ 
iti pippalādiśāntigaṇaḥ 
AVParis gane yad iti pañca sūktāni pañcāpatyāni bhavanti pāñcajanyāni bhavanti pāñcāpatyo gaṇaḥ 
iti pañcāpatyagaṇaḥ 
 AVParis ambayo yanti śambhumayobhubhyāṃ brahma jajñānam asya vāmasya yo rohita ud asya krtavo mūrdhāham iti dve sūkte viṣāsahim iti  
salilagaṇaḥ  
iti salilagaṇaḥ 
AVParis ye triṣaptā iti viśvakarmā gaṇaḥ 
AVParis aghadviṣṭā devajātā śaṃ no devī varaṇo vārayātai pippalī vidradhasya yā babhrava iti gaṇakarmā gaṇo bhaisajyaś ca bhavati
iti bhaiṣajyagaṇaḥ 
AVParis ayaṃ te yonir ā no bhara dhītī vā ya ity arthasūktam utthāpano gaṇaḥ 
ity utthāpanagaṇaḥ 
AVParis ambayo yanti śambhumayobhū hiraṇyavarṇā niḥsālāṃ ye agnayo brahma
jajñānam ity ekaita devā mṛgārasūktāny uttamaṃ varjayitvāpa naḥ śośucad aghaṃ punantu
mā sasruṣīr himavataḥ pra sravanti vāyog pūtaḥ pavitreṇa śaṃ ca no mayaś ca no 'naḍudbhyas
tvaṃ mahyam āpo vaiśvānaro raśmibhir yamo mṛtyur viśvajit saṃjñānaṃ no yady antarikṣe
punar maitv indriyaṃ śivā naḥ śaṃ no vāto vātu agniṃ brūmo vanaspatīn iti śāntigaṇaḥ 
iti sarvaiḥ sūktaiḥ kauśikoktabṛhacchāntigaṇaḥ 
AVParis ambayo yanti śambhumayobhū hiraṇyavarṇā uta devā yady antarikṣe punar
naitv indriyaṃ śivā naḥ śaṃ no vāto vātv agniṃ brūmo vanaspatīn iti śāntātīyo laghuśāntigaṇaḥ 
 AVParis ye triṣaptā mamāgne varcaḥ prātar agniṃ girāv aragarāṭeṣu divas pṛthivyā hastivarcasaṃ siṃhe vyāghre yaśo havir yas te gandha  
iti tisṛbhir varcasyagaṇaḥ  
AVParis yā asurā manuṣyā mā no vidan namo devavadhebhya ity abhayagaṇaḥ 
AVParis bhūto bhūteṣv iti rājānam abhiṣekagaṇaḥ 
AVParis ya āśānām āśāpālebhyo agner manva iti sapta sūktāni yā oṣadhayaḥ
somarājñīr vaiśvānaro na ā gamac chumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī yad arvācīnam agniṃ brūmo
vanaspatīn iti muñcantu nā bhavāśārvā yā devīr yan mātalī rathakrītam ity etāś catasro
varjayitvā aṃholiṅgagaṇaḥ 
Pariśiṣṭa ghṛtakambalam
AVParis oṃ brahmaṇe brahmavedāya namaskṛtvā svayaṃbhuve 
ghṛtakambalaṃ pravakṣyāmi brahmaṇo nigado yathā 
AVParis bṛhaspatir mahendrāya cakāra ghṛtakambalam 
AVParis athendro ha vā asuraiḥ parājitaś cintām āpede
AVParis taṃ savitābravīt prāyaścittaṃ kuruṣvāpratiruddho bhaviṣyasīti
AVParis tam indro 'bravīt 
bhagavan tvam evāpratiruddhaḥ prāyaścittaṃ kurv iti 
AVParis sa prāyaścittam akarot
AVParis puṇye nakṣatre bārhaspatye muhūrte 'bhijity audumbaraṃ kumbhaṃ droṇena
sāḍhakena pūrayitvā tasminn eva vāsaprabhṛtayaḥ oṣadhayo darbhaprabhṛtayaś ca bilvagaurasarṣapāś
cety etān saṃbhārān saṃbhṛtya ghṛtakumbhaṃ barhiṣy ādhāyaitair gaṇair ājyaṃ juhuyāt 
AVParis pra pateta ity ekenāṅgādaṅgāc chamalam avalikhya sapatnaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ
hṛdaye imarmaṇi vāsināvidhya gomayena kāṣāyeṇa vācchādya śānter apratighātakaṃ karma
tato jyeṣṭhaṃ ghṛtakambalaṃ brahmaṇaḥ putram akarot
AVParis tasya ha vā etasya ghṛtakambalasya sāvitrīgaṇaśarīrasya śantātīyaḥ
śiraḥ triṣaptīyo mukhaṃ rudraraudrau cakṣuṣī ghṛtaliṅga āsyaṃ nairṛto jihvā dantoṣṭhāv
abhayāparājitau kṛtyādūṣaṇacātanau śrotre śarmavarmasvastyayanau bāhū mātṛnāmavāṣṭoṣpatyau
pādaupāyuś ca bhaiṣajyaṃ nyāyaḥ prāṇāpānāv iti mīmāṃsata ity
 AVParis eṣa ha vai jyeṣṭho ghṛtakambalo brahmaṇaḥ putro 'parājitagaṇeneṣṭvendro 'surān ajayan mṛtyum alakṣmīm arātiṃ duḥsvapnadurbhūtāny 
AVParis yathā caivaṃvidvān ghṛtakambalaṃ kurute sarvakāmān āpnoti sarvavyādhirahito bhavati brahmalokam avāpnotīti brāhmaṇam 
AVParis yadā sarvam idaṃ vyāptam asurair nāvaśeṣitam 
sthātuṃ devāḥ parābhūtās te 'tharvāṇam upāgatāḥ

AVParis iti bruvatyaḥ sarvās tā yatra homaḥ kṛto bhavet

AVParis lakṣajāpottaraṃ gatvā nadīm udadhigāminīm

AVParis tato māṇḍaliko rājā dīnārāṇāṃ gavāṃ śatam

Pariśiṣṭa samuccayaprāyaścittāni
resembles in form the th adhyāya of the Kauśikasūtra
AVParis oṃ bhṛgvaṅgirorūpadhāriṇe śivāya namaḥ 
atha yatraitad apahanyamāne musalaṃ patati tad ghoraṃ bhavati tad apy etad ṛcoktam 
AVParis ulūlhalān musalaṃ patitaṃ hinasti patnīṃkule jyeṣṭham

AVParis yadvat prajāḥ papanayad dhastād yadi volūkhalāt

AVParis vajro 'si sapatnaheti tisraḥ 
AVParis vajro 'si sapatnahā tvayādya vṛtraṃ sākṣīya

AVParis mekhalādīni cet plaveran punar upanayeta

Pariśiṣṭa brahmakūrcavidhiḥ
AVParis oṃ brahmakūrcavidhiṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkṣepād vacmy asaṃśayam 
pāvanānāṃ paraṃ yo hi pāvanaṃ tapasāṃ tapaḥ

Pariśiṣṭa varṇapaṭalam
AVParis oṃ varṇān pūrvaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ prākṛtā ye ca vaikṛtāḥ 
śrutinirvacanāt sarve vivadante vivṛttiṣu 
AVParis vṛttiḥ karaṇaṃ varṇānāṃ karṇayos tu śrutir yathā 
śrutipradeśād vimatas tad yathā varṇa ucyate 
AVParis samānasaṃdhyakṣarāṇi sparśā antaḥsthā ūṣmāṇaḥ 
etair anye na dṛśyante etāvān varṇasaṃcayaḥ 
AVParis yeṣāṃ ca śrutisaṃhitāyāṃ vibhāge asadṛśī syāt 
tān eva varnān virudrādaye ca pradise kṛtaḥ 
AVParis ye varṇābhyāṃ śrūyante ca yeṣāṃ nāsti vibhāgataḥ 
mānasāṃś cāpi saṃgrāhyān upadeśena vartayet 
AVParis krāntān bahir nidhānasya yamāṃś cānanunāsikān 
savyākṣepaṃ tato varṇān upadeśena vartayet 
AVParis iti varṇāḥ svarāḥ proktās teṣām ādyāś caturdaśa 
samānākṣarāṇy ucyante śeṣaḥ saṃdhyakṣarāṇi tu 
AVParis anavarṇasvaro nāmi kādayo vyañjanaṃ smṛtam 
pañcaviṃśatir ādyaiṣāṃ sparśā vargāś ca pañcakāḥ 
AVParis catvāro yādayo 'ntaḥsthāḥ śādir ūṣmāṣṭako gaṇaḥ 
ayogavāhā vartante teṣām ādyāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ 
AVParis visarjanīyo 'nusvāro jigvāmūlīya ity adhaḥ 
upadhmānīya ity ete catvāro 'tha pare yamāḥ 
AVParis nāsikyābhinidhānau ca vidyate yena pūraṇam 
pañcaṣaṣṭir iyān vāco rāśir yo vedalokayoḥ 
AVParis mukhanāsike ye varṇā ucyante te 'nunāsikāḥ 
samānāsyaprayatnā ye te savarṇā iti smṛtāḥ 
AVParis hrasvo 'varṇaparas tasya savarṇasya ca vācakaḥ 
hrasvottaras tu dīrgho 'pi tasmāt tasmāt tasyaiva vācakaḥ 
AVParis vargāntaras tu vargādir vargasya grāhako mataḥ 
vargāṇāṃ ca yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prathamāditvam iṣyate 
AVParis akāreṇocyate 'tas tu kāro yasmāt paro bhavet 
tasya tad grahaṇaṃ bodhyaṃ kakāro 'tra nidarśanam 
AVParis vyañjanaṃ ghoṣavatsaṃjñam antaḥsthā haḥ parau yamau 
trayastrayaś ca vargāntyā agoṣaḥ śeṣa ucyate 
AVParis śaṣasāś ca yamau dvau ca dvitīyāḥ prathamāś ca ye 
aghoṣā vyañjanaśeṣaṃ ghoṣavad dṛśyate budhaiḥ 
AVParis ataḥ sthānāni varṇānāṃ kaṇṭho 'varṇahakārayoḥ 
vosarjanīya ai au ca svādyayor mātrayoḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVParis śeṣas tālvoṣṭhayor bodhyaḥ sa yathāsaṃkhyam iṣyate 
dvisthānaṃ yamayoś cāpi vargāntyānāṃ ca śiṣyate 
AVParis jihvāmūlām ṛvarṇasya kavargasya ca bhāṣyate 
yaś caiva jihvāmūlīya Lvarṇaś ceti ca smṛtaḥ 
AVParis tālv eyaśacavargāṇām ivarṇasya ca bhāṣyate

AVParis dantā lasatavargāṇām uvarṇas tv oṣṭhya ucyate 
upadhmānīya okāro vaḥ pavargaś ca tathā matāḥ 
AVParis nāsikye nāsikā sthānaṃ tathānusvāra iṣyate 
yamā vargottamāś cāpi yathoktaṃ caiva te matāḥ 
AVParis rephasya dantamūlāni pratyag vā tebhya iṣyate 
iti sthānāni varṇānāṃ kīrtitāni yathākramam

AVParis dhūmrābho lāṅgalasthāyī śrīmān salakṣmamaṇḍalaḥ 
pakṣādau yadi dṛśyeta brahmakṣatrasukhāvaḥ 
AVParis rājavīthīṃ tu saṃprāpta ugradaṇḍī yadā bhavet 
haridrākuṅkumābhaś ca śmaśānam avalokayet 
AVParis mṛtyuṃ saṃyojayet somo bālākṛtir avāṅchirāḥ 
lākṣārudhirasaṃkāśo dhanuḥsthāyī yadā bhavet 
AVParis saṃgrāmaṃ yojayet somo loke tu tumulaṃ bhayam 
dvicandraṃ gaganaṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād brahmavadho mahān 
AVParis dvau sūryau vā yadā syātāṃ tadā kṣatravadho mahān 
dṛṣṭvā tu caturaḥ sūryān uditān sarvatodiśam 
AVParis śastreṇa janamāreṇa tad yugāntasya lakṣaṇam 
āditye pāṇḍuraṃ chattraṃ saṃdhyāvelāṃ yadā bhavet 
AVParis deśasya vidravaṃ sūryo rājamṛtyuṃ vinirdiśet 
ādityasya rathaḥ śvetaḥ saṃdhyāvelāṃ yadā bhavet 
AVParis pratyāsannaṃ bhayaṃ vidyāt tasminn utpātadarśane 
AVParis ādityaḥ sarvataś chinno dvaidhībhutaḥ pradṛśyate deśasya vidravaṃ sūryo rājamṛtyuṃ vinirdiśet 
AVParis kṣemaṃ vikukṣile brūyāt sthālīpiṭharasaṃsthite 
saṃkṣipte kṣīyate loko durbhikṣaṃ vajrasaṃsthite 
AVParis divā hy asmin pataty ulkā satataṃ kampate mahī 
aparvāśaninirghoṣāḥ saṃdhyā ca jvalanacchavā 
AVParis nakṣatrapātasyotpattir dhūmasya rajaso 'pi vā 
śṛṅgaṃ bhavaty ādityasya tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca śuṣyati 
AVParis rājāno hy aśivās tatra citraṃ varṣati mādhavaḥ 
dvādaśānāṃ tu māsānāṃ madhye naśyati pārthivaḥ 
AVParis kārttikyāṃ śuklapakṣasya bahulasya trayodaśīm 
vidyāt tu svātisaṃpātaṃ divasān ekaviṃśatim 
AVParis saptāhaṃ tu bhaved goṣu saptāhaṃ mṛgapakṣiṣu 
mānuṣeṣu ca saptāhaṃ tataḥ śreyas tu kalpayet 
Pariśiṣṭa grahayuddham
AVParis oṃ ke cid grahā nārarān āśrayante ke cid grahā jyotiṣi saṃgrahe ca 
graho graheṇaiva hataḥ kathaṃ syād vijñāya tattvaṃ bhagavān bravītu 
AVParis evaṃ sa pṛṣṭo munibhir mahātmā provāca gargo grahayuddhatantram 
parājayaṃ caiva jayaṃ ca teṣāṃ śubhāsubhamaśubhamñ
caiva jagaddhitāya 
AVParis arko jātaḥ kaliṅgeṣu yavaneṣu ca candramāḥ 
aṅgārakas tv avantyāyāṃ magadhāyāṃ budhas tathā 
AVParis bṛhaspatiḥ saindhaveṣu mahārāṣṭre tu bhārgavaḥ 
śanaiścaraḥ surāṣṭrāyāṃ rāhus tu giriśṛṅgajaḥ 
ketur malayake jāta ity etad grahajātakam 
AVParis yasmin deśe tu yo jātaḥ sa grahaḥ pīḍyate yadā taṃ deśaṃ ghātitaṃ vidyād durbhikṣeṇa bhayena vā 
AVParis divākaraś caiva śanaiścaras tathā bṛhaspatiś caiva budhaś ca nāgarāḥ 
prajāpatiḥ ketur athāpi candramās tathaiva rāhūśanasau ca yāyinaḥ 
AVParis yadā graho nagara eva nāgaraṃ vijeṣyate yāyy atha vāpi yāyinam 
tadā nṛpo nāgara eva nāgaraṃ vijeṣyate vāyy atha vāpi yāyinam 
AVParis ārohaṇaṃ ca bhedaś ca lekhanaṃ savyadakṣiṇam 
raśmisaṃsarjanaṃ caiva grahayuddhaṃ caturvidham 
AVParis prasavye vigrahaṃ brūyāt saṃgrāmaṃ raśmisaṃgame 
lekhane 'mātyapūḍā syād bhedane tu janakṣayaḥ 
AVParis sarveṣāṃ nabhasi samāgame grahāṇām uktṛṣṭo bhavati tathaiva raśmivān yaḥ 
snigdhatvaṃ bhavati tu yasya sa graho graheṇa saṃyukto bhavati tu yaḥ parājayeta śeṣaḥ 
AVParis śyāmo vā vyapagataraśmimaṇḍalo vā rūkṣo vā vyapagataraśmivān kṛśo vā 
ākrānto vinipatitas tato 'pasavyo vijñeyo hata iti sa graho graheṇa 
AVParis budhaś ca bhaumaḥ śanibhārgavāṅgirāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ yāti yadā niśākaram 
anamayatvaṃ triṣu saukhyam uttamaṃ viparyaye cāpi mahāñ janakṣayaḥ 
AVParis dhanakanakarajatasaṃcayāś ca sarve śamadamamantraparāś caye manuṣyāḥ 
śakayavanatukhārabālhikāś ca kṣayam upayānti divākarasya ghāte 
AVParis atha some hate vidyād dhrvaṃ rājño viparyayaḥ 
saṃharanti ca bhūtāni bhūmipālāḥ pṛthakpṛthak 
AVParis parasparaṃ virudhyante kṣudbhayaṃ cāpi dāruṇām 
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ vidyāt somaviparyaye 
AVParis traigartāḥ kṣitipatayaḥ sayodhamukhyāḥ pīḍyante girinilayāgnijīvinaś ca 
saṃgrāmāḥ sarudhirapāṃsuvarṣamiśrā durbhikṣaṃ bhavati dharāsutasya ghāte 
AVParis sāgaranilayāḥ paurāḥ kṣayam upayānti narā vaṇikpradhānāḥ 
bhavati tu rājā vijayī prayāyī budhabandhane prapatanti cātra sobhyāḥ 
AVParis daivajñās tapasi ciraṃ suniścitārthāḥ syur dāntā nṛpatigaṇaḥ purohitāś ca 
āgantur jayati vadhaś ca nāgarāṇāṃ trailokyam  ca
bhayam upaiti guros tu ghāte 
AVParis yo rājā prathitaparākramaḥ pṛthivyāṃ vaṅgāṅgādiṣu madadhāḥ saśūrasenāḥ 
ye yodhāḥ samaraṇabhumilabdhaśabdās te sainyaiḥ kṣayam upayānti śukraghāte 
AVParis mahiṣakavṛṣabhāḥ sabhasmapauṇḍrāḥ kṛṣipaśupālyaratāś ca ye manuṣyāḥ 
vividhabhayasamāhitās tu sarve kṣayam upayānti śanaiścarasya ghāte 
AVParis ye ke cin nṛpatiṣu dāmbhikāḥ piśācāḥ kāryāṇāṃ vrataniyameṣu channapāpāḥ 
ye cānye śabarapulindacedigādhā bādhyante yadi bhavate 'tra rāhughātaḥ 
AVParis ākrāntaṃ samanubhavanti yāyisaṃghā vadhyante yadi bhavate paras paro 'highātaḥ 
saṃgrāmāḥ sarudhirapāṃsuvarṣamiśra durbhikṣaṃ bhavati tu ketupīḍanena 
AVParis yat kiṃ cid divigatam antarikṣajaṃ vā bhaumaṃ vā bhavati nimittam apraśastam 
tat savaṃ stanitamahābhrabidyudvarṣaiḥ śāntaṃ syād bhavati sadakṣiṇaiś ca homaiḥ 
AVParis ye deśā grahagaṇabhinnabhūmikampā yeṣāṃ vā graha upayātacandrasūryaḥ 
tān deśān grahagaṇabhinnabhumikampān parjanyaḥ śamayati saptarātravṛṣṭyā 
AVParis prasavyas triṣu māseṣu saṃsargo māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ 
lekhane pakṣa ity āhur bhedane saptarātrikam 
AVParis āgneyā vāsavāś caiva vāyavyā vāruṇās tathā 
sarva eva śubhā jñeyā gargasya vacanaṃ yathā 
Pariśiṣṭa grahasaṃgrahaḥ
AVParis om atharvāṇaṃ namaskṛtya uvāca bhagavān ṛṣiḥ 
kīdṛśā grahaputrāś ca kiyanto vā vadasva me 
AVParis pṛṣṭaha sa śaunakenātha brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya vai 
saṃkhyām uvāca bhagavān padmayonimataṃ yathā 
AVParis dikcāriṇo divicarā bhūcarā vyomacāriṇaḥ 
divācarā rātricarā divārātricarāś caye 
AVParis pṛthikcarāś ca ye tatra te ca syuḥ saṃghacāriṇaḥ 
caranty aparavīthīṣu ye ca vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ 
AVParis te grahāḥ saṃgraheṇāhaṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ 
anekavidhasaṃsthānaṃ pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ 
AVParis gokṣīrakumudaprakhyās tīvreṇa vapuṣānvitāḥ 
caranty antaravīthīṣu snigdhā vipulatejasaḥ 
AVParis ete visarpakā nāma arciṣmanto mahāprabhāḥ 
vijñeyāś caturaśītiḥ śukraputrā mahāgrahāḥ 
AVParis śuklā nikarāḥ saurābhās tyajanta iva cārciṣaḥ

AVParis prāyaśo dakṣiṇe mārge nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ 
vikacāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭis te bṛhaspatisutāḥ smṛtaḥ 
AVParis ye śvetāḥ kiṃcid ākṛṣṇā viśikhāḥ syur vitārakāḥ

AVParis ekapaKcāśato jñeyās taskarāḥ sūkṣmaraśmayaḥ

AVParis kauṅkumā lohitāṅgasya putrā vidrumatejasaḥ

AVParis nānādhūmanibhā rūkṣā dhūmavyākularaśmayaḥ

AVParis kṛṣṇābhāḥ kṛṣṇaparyantāḥ kaluṣākṛtiraśmayaḥ 
rāhoḥ putrās trayas triṃśad grahās tāmasakīlakāḥ 
AVParis nānāvarṇāgnisaṃkāśā jvālāmālā visarpiṇaḥ 
viśvarūpāḥ sutā agner grahā viṃśaṃ śataṃ smṛtam 
AVParis aruṇās tu sutā vāyor dāruṇāḥ saptasaptatiḥ 
vāteritā bhramantīva rūkṣā vikīrṇaraśmayaḥ 
AVParis tārāpuñjapratīkāśās tārāmaṇḍalasaṃvṛtāḥ

AVParis catvāras tārajā yuktāḥ sūkṣmāṇo rūparaśmayaḥ 
brahmasaṃtānakā nāma dve śate caturuttare 
AVParis vaṃśagulmapratīkāśā vaṃśagulmasaraśmayaḥ 
kākatuṇḍanibhābhiś ca raśmibhiḥ kiṃcid āvṛtāḥ 
AVParis udakaṃ cotsṛjantīva snigdhatvāt saumyadarśanāḥ 
ete nāmnā smṛtāḥ kaṅkās triṃśad dvau vāruṇā grahāḥ 
AVParis muṇḍatārāḥ kabandhābhā rukmakeśāś ca raśmayaḥ 
kālaputrāḥ kabandhās te smṛtāḥ ṣaṇṇavatir grahāḥ 
AVParis arciṣmāṃś ca prabhāsaś ca romaśo viṣamāṃs tathā

AVParis ṛṣakaiś caiva rādhātaḥ kumudaḥ phanako ghanaḥ

AVParis nakṣatracāriṇo hy ete bhṛguputrā mahābalāḥ

AVParis atisaṃtānakāś tv anye ṣaṣṭir vāyoḥ sutā grahāḥ

AVParis miśrībhūtās tu te jñeyā guṇṭhitā iva reṇunā

AVParis atyarthaṃ kanakās tv anye prataptakanakaprabhāḥ

AVParis ye tu nakṣatravaṃśasya bhāgam uttaram āśritāḥ

AVParis vyālakasya tu ye putrāḥ saptaṣaṣṭiḥ samantataḥ

AVParis saṃtānakanibhā ye tu dṛśyante sūkṣmaraśmayaḥ

AVParis brahmarāśes tu te putrā grahāḥ saṃtānasaṃsthitāḥ

AVParis aṇavo lohitās tv anye prakāśante 'dhikeśakāḥ

AVParis pariveṣeṣu jāteṣu grahāṇāṃ maṇḍaleṣu ca

AVParis adharmasaṃbhavās tv anye caturdaśa parikramāḥ 
adhaḥśikhāḥ prakāśante vivarṇā ghoratārakāḥ

AVParis vajraḥ kavandhas triśirāḥ śaṅkhabhedī śikhāvataḥ

AVParis yathā somārkayor jyoter maṇḍalābhyāśasevinaḥ

AVParis tatra mandaphalā jñeyāḥ śaśāṅkatalasevinaḥ 
divākaratalābhyāśaṃ sevino bhṛśadāruṇāḥ 
AVParis pannagās tu caturviṃśat kṛṣṇā dvātriṃśatir grahāḥ 
dakṣiṇādyāsu vīkṣyante nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ 
AVParis kevalaṃ tārakākārā dṛśyante niḥprabhaprabhāḥ

AVParis dakṣiṇāparataś cāpi pītaraktau grahau smṛtau

AVParis aiśānyāṃ śvetaraktābha ekas tiṣṭhati sūryakaḥ 
yaḥ saṃdhivelāsv arkābho dikṣu sarvāsu dṛśyate 
AVParis nātidūre raveḥ snigdhaḥ sa varṣāyābhayāya ca

AVParis karṇaś ca raibhyasya putrau cārvāvasuparāvasū

AVParis sthāvarāṇāṃ narendrāṇāṃ prācyānāṃ pakṣam āśritāḥ

AVParis śiśumāreṇa sahitā dhruveṇa ca mahātmanā

AVParis hāhāhūhū ca vijñeyau viṣṇoś ca padam uttamam

AVParis kūṭasthānāni sarvāṇi dikṣv etāny upadhārayet

AVParis śikhāḥ sṛjanto vitatās tantuśuklapaṭopamāḥ

AVParis uddālakarṣiputrās te nīcair vibhrāntamaṇḍalāḥ

AVParis viraśmayaś ca viśikhā mahākāyā nirarciṣaḥ

AVParis bhūmyām abhyuditā vā syur hrasvasnehapariplutāḥ

AVParis sarveṣāṃ paitṛkaṃ karma prajābhāgyodbhavaṃ mahat

AVParis tatkarmajanmamāhātmyaṃ śīlābhijanam eva ca

AVParis sarva eva rogapradā mṛtyuśastrāgnitaskaraiḥ

AVParis dhūpanāt sparśanāt sthānād udayāstamasaṃbhavāt

AVParis mṛdudhruvograkṣipreṣu sādhāraṇacareṣu ca

AVParis yathādiṣṭaṃ yathāvarṇaṃ yathāvargaparigraham

AVParis mṛtyoḥ kālasya sūryasya brahmaṇas tryambakasya ca

AVParis prajāpateś ca dharmasya somasya varuṇasya ca

AVParis kaśyapasya ca marīcer uddālakaṛṣes tathā

AVParis śukrādīnāṃ ca ye putrā grahāṇāṃ parikīrtitāḥ

AVParis nāradātreyagargāṇāṃ guror uśanasas tathā

AVParis anekaśatasāhasra anekaśatalakṣaṇaḥ

AVParis etadutthe tu sarvasmin bhaye 'tha samupasthite
